<h1 class="devsite-page-title" style="width:50%" id="wear-compose" data-text="Wear Compose" tabindex="-1">Wear Compose</h1>




  



  






  




<div style="align:right; text-align:right; padding-bottom:21px; margin-top:-45px; border-bottom:1px solid black;"> 
&nbsp;&nbsp;
</div>



<div style="float:left; font-size:medium; margin-bottom:5px; margin-top:10px" class="nocontent">
<div style="text-align:left; font-size:90%; padding-right:30px; margin-right:10px; margin-bottom:10px;"> 
API Reference<br>

<a href="/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/material/package-summary">androidx.wear.compose.material</a><br>

</div>
</div>

<div style="text-align:left; padding-left:10px; margin-left:10px; margin-top:15px; margin-bottom:10px;">


Write Jetpack Compose applications for Wearable devices by
providing functionality to support wearable specific devices, sizes, shapes and
navigation gestures.

</div>



<div style="clear:both"></div>









<table style="width:100%">
<tr>
<th style="width:15%">Latest Update</th>
<th style="width:15%">Stable Release</th>
<th style="width:15%">Release Candidate</th>
<th style="width:15%">Beta Release</th>
<th style="width:15%">Alpha Release</th></tr>

<tr>

<td>December 11, 2024</td>


<td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/wear-compose#1.4.0">1.4.0</a></td>



<td>-</td>




<td>-</td>




<td><a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/wear-compose#1.5.0-alpha07">1.5.0-alpha07</a></td>


</tr>
</table>



<h2 id="declaring_dependencies" data-text="Declaring dependencies" tabindex="-1">Declaring dependencies</h2>

<p>To add a dependency on Wear, you must add the Google Maven repository to your
project. Read <a href="/studio/build/dependencies#google-maven">Google&#39;s Maven repository</a>
for more information.</p>

<p>Add the dependencies for the artifacts you need in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">build.gradle</code> file for
your app or module:</p>























































































<div>
<div class="ds-selector-tabs"><section><h3 id="groovy" data-text="Groovy" tabindex="-1">Groovy</h3>
<div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Groovy"><span class="devsite-syntax-n">dependencies</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">implementation</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.4.0"</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// For Wear Material Design UX guidelines and specifications</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">implementation</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.4.0"</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// For integration between Wear Compose and Androidx Navigation libraries</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">implementation</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.4.0"</span>

<h2 id="wear_compose_material3_version_10_2" data-text="Wear Compose Material3 Version 1.0" tabindex="-1">Wear Compose Material3 Version 1.0</h2>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha30" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha30" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha30</h3>

<p>December 11, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha30</code> is released. Version 1.0.0-alpha30 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6f09cf2ae979e48fdb19485f757a033e4a34bb82..46295bc0b75a16f452e8e0090e8de41073d4dbb6/wear/compose/compose-material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">scrollTransform</code> modifier for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> was refactored which triggered an API change. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0c6dc9a7ab2a12a3ebf33f822179145a9ba4c7d9">I0c6dc</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconToggleButtonShapes</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextToggleButtonShapes</code> to have two different shape parameters <code translate="no" dir="ltr">uncheckedPressed</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">checkedPressed</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I85dbd069e3de01b50deac5d923bebfc2d081e6fd">I85dbd</a>)</li>
<li>Invalid month/day options are now visible in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code>, with a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">invalidPickerContentColor</code>, when using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">minDate</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">maxDate</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If4541e0c2d64ab0a94e11a1bda6efa1277f8ddbc">If4541</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> API to provide <code translate="no" dir="ltr">increaseIcon</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">decreaseIcon</code> slots - the content for these can be built as usual from the Icon composable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id35dad8eb3829a80c6acf46d7a7ae9650bcbfbac">Id35da</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">dynamicColorScheme</code> by removing the optional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">defaultColorScheme</code> parameter and now returning nullable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ColorScheme</code>. This means that the caller must explicitly handle the fallback case when a dynamic color scheme is not provided. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6d62ea8d01175b2a95772b771a469bed96071231">I6d62e</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the icon sizes in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonDefaults</code> for use with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code>. A <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> containing only an icon should use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonDefaults.SmallIconSize = 24.dp</code>, whereas a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> containing both icon and text should use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonDefaults.ExtraSmallIconSize = 20.dp</code>. It is recommended that <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> wrap its content (rather than filling the max width) and samples have been updated to show that. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0582cad17c66743a1df5d87adbe2cf89b6fda8fb">I0582c</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButtonDefaults</code> with recommended icon sizes for the 4 different <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButtonSizes</code>. Also, updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code> layout so that it has slightly larger bottom padding than top padding, which improves appearance for both Icon and Text content. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id772a6ba9f0259c50daad54a8a701fcfd3d3d68f">Id772a</a>)</li>
<li>We have added motion to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LinearProgressIndicator</code> and exposed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LinearProgressIndicatorContent</code> which provides the visual content without animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idee9941c34444a2a695a0ab2171306085b7d5abd">Idee99</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CircularProgressIndicatorContent</code> composable to display the visual content of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CircularProgressIndicator</code> without animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie33d4492d0d1f15dac976716760d6e118c5f5e8e">Ie33d4</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> newly provides the composition  local <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTransformingLazyColumnItemScope</code> which <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Card</code>s, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button</code>s and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader</code>s now use to automatically morph when placed inside a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code>. Callers can disable automatic morphing using the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformExclusion</code> wrapper.  (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1652f87699096f3de1cef247d714099a105647a2">I1652f</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the type of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonDefaults.shape</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RoundedCornerShape</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iccdf254dc1f3eb838d7098638666fcbf1ebdfb85">Iccdf2</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug to respect existing alpha on background for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1eb60d1ba1b165c5cb65c2c2400ac860cb8b884c">I1eb60</a>)</li>
<li>We have set <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextMotion</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Animated</code> by default in our typography, to avoid text jitter due to snapping letter glyphs to pixel boundaries during scaling operations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I626fa13dd827e62311e51e7ccd49eda3e53e06f7">I626fa</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the appearance of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code> by increasing width and gap size, to improve visibility. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ied7cbcd23d60b53b57d338ad5033b8de8208e688">Ied7cb</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.scrollTransform</code> when adding/removing/moving items. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6830fe9d9df3645a822eb3e1b352aad1a1def2d6">I6830f</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a round button animation issue for short taps (previously, the minimum animation duration was not always observed). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I757a7bd0f4c8b07572b8a5d24d5660cde6648ff6">I757a7</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the sweep angle for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LevelIndicator</code> to 20% (i.e. 72 degrees). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idde5c5cfcda06eab99079a285eb8132ff4f13751">Idde5c</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code> positioning when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> was used with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AutoCenteringParams</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I387dd3de162e485d0c5658dbb383a888dc9ed05c">I387dd</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the colors and typography for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListSubHeader</code>. Also the colors for the toggle controls on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CheckboxButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwitchButton</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3981715cfd1073a43a574d61ed7249c6a02221e3">I39817</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code> positioning in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ContentPadding</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2bc51a0d5b12916e3d560bf9b2e9119601fb21a9">I2bc51</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug seen in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OpenOnPhoneDialog</code> progress animation by using the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CircularProgressIndicatorContent</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3e44325b2c452fd2f86b26affcd727ed416e2973">I3e443</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPagerScaffold</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalPagerScaffold</code> to disable animations when reduce motion is enabled (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaaf681ea58b2869a5911a6878af82061bc939b64">Iaaf68</a>)</li>
<li>We have implemented a separate animation for circular progress indicators when progress reaches over 100%. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4713589deb69b42502b799d921ef38a2ffc04ec0">I47135</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code> could be drawn with an incorrect shape in Pager components (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I91db9e462a13e348e4b3a7ca1a6610fcbb4c9898">I91db9</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha29" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha29" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha29</h3>

<p>November 13, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha29</code> is released. Version 1.0.0-alpha29 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ccd90a76bd7c4acf4f4f01eca76350e383bc441e..6f09cf2ae979e48fdb19485f757a033e4a34bb82/wear/compose/compose-material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> to provide default content that shows the time. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id23b37f88d2ad6696cd61d8d9cfa4c04fd634049">Id23b3</a>)</li>
<li>We have simplified the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollInfoProvider</code> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PagerState</code> by removing the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">orientation</code> parameter, which is no longer needed. The new behavior is for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> to remain in place for both horizontal and vertical paging. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I71767df0f68f4109e8ac79aa37a075ff4b3179a3">I71767</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalHapticFeedback</code> now provides a default <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HapticFeedback</code> implementation when the Vibrator API indicates that haptics are supported. The following have been added to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HapticFeedbackType</code> - <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Confirm</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ContextClick</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GestureEnd</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GestureThresholdActivate</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Reject</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SegmentFrequentTick</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SegmentTick</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleOn</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleOff</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VirtualKey</code>.  Wear Compose long-clickable components such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Card</code> now perform the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LONG_PRESS</code> haptic when a long-click handler has been supplied. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5083db2ce3619189c0a3793de9f535d996029c75">I5083d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the motion for Confirmations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I04bff60587cdf8dcfd8dc23635382782e0bd4d6f">I04bff</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the minimum API dependency to 1.7.4 for Compose libraries. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I88b4613796d9c9ccccf3f3a1cf0efd3ad6ce2f41">I88b46</a>)</li>
<li>New motion was added for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OpenOnPhone</code> dialog. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1e10ae52bb6b2da225d203a116a9ce08675b3837">I1e10a</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LevelIndicator</code> so that it is now correctly displayed with the level is zero. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie95a40b1e91275ba029319abcf239ec7a97083a5">Ie95a4</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPageIndicator</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalPageIndicator</code> animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5c8f3f73ff70f71f6821de7a018c1cf084548091">I5c8f3</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a shrink-to-dot animation to the indeterminate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ArcProgressIndicator</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9fd5148d52540ba920d39dd7c1fa187a98382b7c">I9fd51</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha28" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha28" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha28</h3>

<p>October 30, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha28</code> is released. Version 1.0.0-alpha28 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/b8a68b0896897fa158508d73a31998a26161d9a7..ccd90a76bd7c4acf4f4f01eca76350e383bc441e/wear/compose/compose-material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added an arc variation on the indeterminate circular progress indicator (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2efc1df6f9cde6bbee25505b0a45c43246de6986">I2efc1</a>)</li>
<li>We have made public the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialogContent</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Dialog</code> composables that make up the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> API, so that it is possible to add customization if necessary (such as customizing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> animation whilst keeping the recommended content layout). In addition, we have added  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Color</code> parameters to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ConfirmButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DismissButton</code> members of  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialogDefaults</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4eb71abb2f29170154475aa707c915b55b2fec0e">I4eb71</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Placeholder</code> API as follows: renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderState.startPlaceholderAnimation</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderState.animatePlaceholder</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderState.isShowContent</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderState.isHidden</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderDefaults.shape</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderDefaults.Shape</code>; renamed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">painter</code> parameter in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">painterWithPlaceholderOverlayBackgroundBrush</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">originalPainter</code>; changed visibility of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderState.placeholderProgression</code> from public to internal and renamed it to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">placeholderShimmerProgression</code>; added placeholder animation duration constants to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderDefaults</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie5a59415e93c4ff0c8f87940ab48990d250941e1">Ie5a59</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code> API as follows: renamed the parameter on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenScaffold</code> from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">bottomButton</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">edgeButton</code>; made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButtonSize</code> a value class. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieef158ef737bf89a3acc22ff7cadf7929672167e">Ieef15</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the visibility of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">copy()</code> to public in wear material3 Colors classes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0287ff4d034bcb64d8ac96e804e288a8d161b7af">I0287f</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added minimum animation duration for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconToggleButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextToggleButton</code> on click (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieb333b849bcf0bd44ce3834cef71428d0aa14055">Ieb333</a>)</li>
<li>Added minimum duration on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code> shape animation (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iebcee6af7d6620af372cb081012085ad8a9bd40b">Iebcee</a>)</li>
<li>Corrected the repeat option state of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3587c44541f655b48bc5240dc47c8a276c7aa38d">I3587c</a>)</li>
<li>Added motion for Alert and Confirmation dialogs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I173b19c21fe1386c0336530ad8b9c881a401e20c">I173b1</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha27" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha27" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha27</h3>

<p>October 16, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha27</code> is released. Version 1.0.0-alpha27 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/b6ae8d0a0e8cd803f7b84f30101eda1af4f1d6b6..b8a68b0896897fa158508d73a31998a26161d9a7/wear/compose/compose-material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenScaffold</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code> following the renaming of Wear Compose Foundation <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0608b1772ce548b97328f4fa888dfd44cb1306ae">I0608b</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">preferredHeight</code> parameter has been renamed to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">buttonSize</code> and its value can only be chosen from 4 constants in the newly introduced <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButtonSize</code> value class. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icdd7064874afdd8c68bd9e97cd936c7b54145559">Icdd70</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the naming of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListSubheader</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListSubHeader</code> and added publicly accessible default values for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListSubHeader</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9673008ab833ca249d445ac3fc240ca8f25e473f">I96730</a>)</li>
<li>We have added new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPagerScaffold</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalPagerScaffold</code> components for Wear which provide new animations and coordination between time text and page indicator components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iff7d026c30a147ca7a40b372dc99cece2ad30665">Iff7d0</a>)</li>
<li>We have added rotary support to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPagerScaffold</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalPagerScaffold</code>, enabling users to navigate pagers using rotary input devices. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9770d94d93d745228694c50c58360c66a4b82257">I9770d</a>)</li>
<li>We have made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MotionScheme</code> API changes to simplify the usage and improve consistency. Removed inlined remember functions and moved the  built-in Motion Schemes to a dedicated MotionScheme companion object. Renamed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">standardMotionScheme</code> and the  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expressiveMotionScheme</code> to standard and expressive. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5fd45ba14b76e5ef417e88b6696183236b83c500">I5fd45</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for a dynamic color scheme based on system colors. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I073e9acdbe246030c7359dc41b8c64bf08ce7199">I073e9</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the Stepper to the latest UX specs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I622bb721b385543e3b9654a049dd42d649176988">I622bb</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated typography and paddings for Card components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3ae48efdb6d3c694c95788cefd2af968fd6fe9e5">I3ae48</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the padding in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> between Confirm/Dismiss buttons and the rest of the content from 8dp to 12dp according to UX specs (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie55f06be54c05b2a5bd229c44729c1358419f4a0">Ie55f0</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the color opacity for the Slider component. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idb383cb774b5d612aaa0d0f63e596625cfaa2d4d">Idb383</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha26" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha26" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha26</h3>

<p>October 2, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha26</code> is released. Version 1.0.0-alpha26 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/0431b84980e97d6bafdfda7c9038bc4d9529564f..b6ae8d0a0e8cd803f7b84f30101eda1af4f1d6b6/wear/compose/compose-material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the API and appearance of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPageIndicator</code> and added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalPageIndicator</code> for use with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalPager</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic9309eb67f73b9d48fcd35087a6452e11f23fa2e">Ic9309</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> now supports the ability to omit the default bottom button from the button stack variation, for custom layouts in which EdgeButton is not required. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I34fa93b55b1041959a6a06f63ee270446992e2be">I34fa9</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> component for Wear Material 3 (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic38b2a0ead09beaf2314b17eb0c02dd2b0f22419">Ic38b2</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for bi-directional swiping in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code>, for rare cases where the current screen does not support swipe to dismiss. The default is still to swipe-to-reveal only on right-to-left swipes and it is strongly advised to respect the default behavior to avoid conflict with swipe to dismiss. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifac04be22f302315ff1cd2160a44c24c82f29612">Ifac04</a>)</li>
<li>We have renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">buttonHeight</code> parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">preferredHeight</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4fab3926384cdff5a82574acfcc8a5ade290539e">I4fab3</a>)</li>
<li>The Kotlin version has been updated to 1.9 (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1a14ce236e70bdc55f94afd42ead44587018c097">I1a14c</a>)</li>
<li>We have renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OpenOnPhoneDialogDefaults.Icon</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OpenOnPhoneDialogDefaults.OpenOnPhoneIcon</code> to avoid clashing with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Icon</code>(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0f391a8945723bc6647ff3f7d6fda97e9e453883">I0f391</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia546a61ed40616d774509a31bce9dc4c6a8ee3f5">Ia546a</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated default values for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextToggleButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconToggleButton</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7aaa9980b8e5d21d8bc44882feebb3a6ee479c1f">I7aaa9</a>)</li>
<li>We have simplified the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Picker</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code> API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id065352238dc9318d7bbb738fd7d7020e9358cdc">Id0653</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.Shape</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.Height</code>, which (being tokens) were otherwise private to developers using the library. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1594a5907bee183eb2183dec2e85e791c6dda3be">I1594a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/347649765">b/347649765</a>)</li>
<li>We have renamed the progress parameter for the binary segmented circular progress indicator to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">segmentValue</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib72d913de07f54a9f7d31fa2c2339a9a4af1491b">Ib72d9</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the colors and layout for Slider. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic3eec615ce17a02b8cb92f253f12fd547ecfdf27">Ic3eec</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">openOnPhone</code> icon animation (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I66f856678de177954c078bfbcf23727befd17939">I66f85</a>)</li>
<li>We are now using Google Symbols icons in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Slider</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePicker</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I46c7ca7f34ae6ed28b76ab28a8c86376a2755d4c">I46c7c</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the paddings in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Confirmation</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OpenOnPhoneDialog</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaa82ee494777b09e4316c486189680c45079518e">Iaa82e</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha25" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha25" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha25</h3>

<p>September 18, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha25</code> is released. Version 1.0.0-alpha25 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/80f82d37cb9b40250ee9eb15d9cbe9e93849355e..0431b84980e97d6bafdfda7c9038bc4d9529564f/wear/compose/compose-material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added an Indeterminate circular progress indicator. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I427a7af6d8e9f7de6465e18f010f4b6880ef0b5a">I427a7</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for progress overflow (&gt;100% progress) for both the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CircularProgressIndicator</code> and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SegmentedCircularProgressIndicator</code>. When the progress exceeds 1.0, this will be indicated by the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">overflowTrack</code> color. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaaa3d4da94307062cd92916be09130bae63afe6a">Iaaa3d</a>)</li>
<li>The round <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconToggleButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextToggleButton</code> now support a new shape animation variation, in which different shapes represent checked, unchecked and pressed states. The earlier animated shape variation for the just pressed state continues to be supported. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I29f033f2f3601c03972252865b8e2da24fb1d630">I29f03</a>)</li>
<li>We have removed support for using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Column</code>, due to the need to specify the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code> height explicitly in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenScaffold</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie353de35ca447165e315638190a30bfb533436ce">Ie353d</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for the Wear Compose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> with our <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenScaffold</code> (and  added an implementation of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollInfoProvider</code> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumnState</code>). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib8d2946c22fe8279d08b0f8fc9029cdf5b8e0423">Ib8d29</a>)</li>
<li>We have combined <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextMaxLines</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextAlign</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextOverflow</code> into a single <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextConfiguration</code> composition local to provide a more scalable solution going forwards. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5edbc2caf74415a7a40b69c8710e059e7d168324">I5edbc</a>)</li>
<li>We have added arc-large as an additional typescale, reserved for short header text strings at the very top or bottom of the screen, like in Confirmation overlays. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I60e3e7a03658230a4f075df55b0e2d2ff0263dc4">I60e3e</a>)</li>
<li>We have added defaults to Button for recommended large and extra large icon sizes and content padding. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I846759e195384b56656feb0244a86ca3bdc7248c">I84675</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the colors for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I483249cc4f80973e2587dac253f4ae93b6c8d078">I48324</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the base Button overloads to be vertically center-aligned for consistency with other overloads. To restore the previous behavior, use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.align</code> from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RowScope</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I66e572d7a2c0f41343cb94276f5bcab1b194b18b">I66e57</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha24" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha24" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha24</h3>

<p>September 4, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha24</code> is released. Version 1.0.0-alpha24 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6a69101fd0edc8d02aa316df1f43e0552fd2d7c4..80f82d37cb9b40250ee9eb15d9cbe9e93849355e/wear/compose/compose-material3">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a Motion scheme into the Material3 theme. This will be used by components across the library to apply animation specifications such as springs for expressive motion. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I54ff3a7cf0cb4d7315a065f691bf2f9d4a4520a7">I54ff3</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AppScaffold</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenScaffold</code> components to the Material3 library, which include functionality to coordinate layering and transitions of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AppScaffold</code> provides a top level of scaffold components that sit on top of all screens. As such, adding <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AppScaffold</code> allows it to remain in place while swiping between screens. Screens can themselves override or hide the time text. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenScaffold</code> provides a slot for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code> and automatically animates the scroll indicator when scrolling, including timeout to hide the scroll indicator after inactivity. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I047d639623ce9c54af9dabd86728107c8e1af422">I047d6</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code> featuring the new Material3 design. It has a fixed thumb size based on initial list contents, in order to avoid size variations when lazy content is loaded into the list. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic228d48ed349dabb9c1fa02b949f07e3a6a4781b">Ic228d</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollAway</code> API such that <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenStage</code> is a value class instead of an enum class, to allow for additional stages to be added as needed going forwards. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I48c9398b577d42c9792009018d8f494e2a33b479">I48c93</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code>, a distinctive Wear-specific button with a shape that follows the curvature of the bottom of the screen (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I16369a6d41fadde897bce87ddd0300caae90fd89">I16369</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a new slot to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenScaffold</code> for a bottom button (such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code>), that will be shown and resized depending on the scrolling content (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I032eb44f3a38f8de3b6c6082babf837ad7df2a2a">I032eb</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.scrollTransform</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.targetMorphingHeight</code> to add Material3 motion effects to items in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie229a1aa8b3411881367fbe1f0c1ee3a57c39c91">Ie229a</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SegmentedCircularProgressIndicator</code> as a variation on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CircularProgressIndicator</code>.  The segmented variation either shows a single progress value across all segments or shows each segment as being on/off. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6e05980ba823f00f8b7640129bbd4fa1c8fcfdd8">I6e059</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LinearProgressIndicator</code> as an alternative to the existing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CircularProgressIndicator</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I891827cc47667308393cfc7766b2d117806ab7f2">I89182</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code>, providing layouts for presenting important prompts to the user. Variations are included for either a pair of confirm/dismiss buttons or a single bottom button (typically an EdgeButton) below a stack of options. Both variations have slots for icon, title and additional text to provide further details. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieb873637e1ce1a554a9ae01c7ab7a72c63650c19">Ieb873</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OpenOnPhoneDialog</code>, which should be used to indicate an action that will continue on the user&#39;s phone. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OpenOnPhoneDialog</code> is dismissed after a specified timeout. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I978fdd711362f808cac89da4c15fce337ed100bc">I978fd</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Confirmation</code>, a dialog component that has slots for an icon and either curved or linear text. Specific variations are provided for success/failure messages. Confirmations are automatically dismissed after a timeout. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib43e8d613847d334bcb079c07806612526f63983">Ib43e8</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a background to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> to mitigate issues where the underlying content and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> overlapped, and obscured the time. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia11fd1c2a41630620c30d4c46b7e8c54fd659691">Ia11fd</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LevelIndicator</code>, which shows the value of a setting such as volume, and can be used with the existing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> component to construct a volume screen. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LevelIndicator</code> is similar to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code>, but is displayed on the opposite side of the screen and has a wider stroke width and different indicator color by default. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8a4ac3d8ee7e06a1d73642aeee731ecc29298220">I8a4ac</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimePicker</code>, with  layouts for 24 hour time (with or without seconds), or 12 hour time with am/pm selection. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia5124f9e5aab57c5f7a530e5ed55184f86fe579d">Ia5124</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code>, with configuration for column ordering (i.e. day-month-year, month-day-year or year-month-day) and optional min/max dates. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibf13b15b750dc02e7c838f5d1791ad446464d5a7">Ibf13b</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a weight parameter to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">text</code> function. In cases where TimeText is made up of more than one text element, this allows control over how the space is distributed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3670007378ce6d66d0d79424a1a95b5b2ac8ca76">I36700</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitRadioButton</code> - these components simplify the previous API by combining both the (Split)<code translate="no" dir="ltr">SelectableButton</code> and the child radio control (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If7ae8389f0315715c3ba00cd97530eca47f15d0d">If7ae8</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CheckboxButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitCheckboxButton</code> - these components simplify the previous API by combining both the (Split)<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code> and the child Checkbox control (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia8f709ffee3fa93d697c945836d59391f4f25bd0">Ia8f70</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwitchButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitSwitchButton</code> - these components simplify the previous API by combining both the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">(Split)ToggleButton</code> and the child Switch control (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0d3491ce1fb05d1fb83dee2538e7613d7938815c">I0d349</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnimatedText</code> documentation to explain overshooting  behavior. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iff30ada5cd37d6818cc3fbbf34abb6302734f11b">Iff30a</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonGroup</code>to combine 2 or 3 buttons such that button presses produce a coordinated animation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie27db2fd01522caa9e8800b7296aaa4335dc14f3">Ie27db</a>)</li>
<li>We have added optional shape animation for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code> when pressed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iffca57bcabad6283f2192fc42101f968caa00e4b">Iffca5</a>)</li>
<li>We have added an additional color variation, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledVariant</code>, to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I65fc3acf7589eacfc2280b028d83d1e352a100cc">I65fc3</a>)</li>
<li>We have added the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">forcedSize</code> parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ImageWithScrimPainter</code>, such that Button image backgrounds now maintain their component size by default. Setting the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">forcedSize = null</code> adopts the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Painter.instrinsicSize</code> instead. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic57af1323c60a68ab6df859c3ecc348163417981">Ic57af</a>)</li>
<li>We have added long-click to Buttons (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib613d75052d7b4d5d85cc1e7dca009505e427f9c">Ib613d</a>)</li>
<li>Long click support has also been added to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I38891ea0c0179d3c6ec380b1af4d00aa216dd347">I38891</a>)</li>
<li>Long click support has been added to Cards. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I305d5005e98ece7424af6d9c690c5c844836ab5e">I305d5</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextMaxLines</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextAlign</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextOverflow</code> as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocals</code> and used them as parameter defaults on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Text</code>. The composition locals can now be used by components such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CheckboxButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwitchButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> to implement UX guidance, but the parameters can be overridden by developers if necessary. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iab841d8adde34a4aa92920e4372ce3493a8d638a">Iab841</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Placeholder</code> to help in masking the content of components like buttons &amp; cards until the data is loaded. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1a5328e0f4fd379b41cbbcea0e44025d3b5ffb2e">I1a532</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconToggleButtonColors</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextToggleButtonColors</code> to replace the now removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButtonColors</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie0bf11419433e68e344e3c8de46d14eba2cb490f">Ie0bf1</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledTonalButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ChildButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> to use the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocals</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextMaxLines</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextAlign</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTextOverflow</code> to implement UX guidance - these parameters can be overridden by developers on Text directly if necessary (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie51f7257db279c736766c451402e7bc94cbc46d2">Ie51f7</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the default stroke width of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LevelIndicator</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">6dp</code> to differentiate it from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollIndicator</code> which has a stroke width of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">4dp</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If6f63990d09de3fa3f00d542eaf404985a2bc68f">If6f63</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed an issue in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> so that larger sweep angles are supported. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie489f0eb36f7f3c0365759baf827a60810d1e8d0">Ie489f</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed an issue during <code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeButton</code> recomposition. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4cdca0c8de8e08928489e9f6d523301a4de3bc75">I4cdca</a>)</li>
<li>Corrected layouts of split toggle buttons when customized content padding is provided. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia33d396d38c2103b22d832152533cf2132660a0d">Ia33d3</a>)</li>
<li>Rounded up small progress values to at least the line width of the progress indicator. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3bd849c3f8c27ea5ba63317907196f2343bdfa47">I3bd84</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha19" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha19" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha19</h3>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha17" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha17" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha17</h3>

<p>February 7, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha17</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/51191bc12f96f233fc08995e1b4e8ff8b88bc7ce..ca2a8cf8da3a3502fccc593974f8085653e38261/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha17 contains these commits.</a></p>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4fe3b136aeb435d35c629e4fa0ab32bd2931b72f">I4fe3b</a>)</li>
<li>We have refactored default patterns for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonColors</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButtonColors</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButtonColors</code> by creating a cached instance internally and reducing the usage of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocal</code>. <h3 id="1.0.0-alpha16" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha16" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha16</h3>

<p>January 24, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha16</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a8915c4ac4e4bfead52d6b42aaffaa87966ab38b..51191bc12f96f233fc08995e1b4e8ff8b88bc7ce/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha16 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code>, which can use the same filled, filled tonal and outlined colors as Button.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I05df080969e73641c71515ef7ae7627fb93360d7">I05df0</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code>/<code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitRadioButton</code> as containers for selection controls, such as the Radio control. This differs from the existing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code> in that <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> is selectable (and operates within a selection group) whereas <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code> is toggleable (and is independent). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I612758b8625c45756e6a56d31c1008daac45fba3">I61275</a>)</li>
<li>We are removing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalContentAlpha</code> from the Wear Compose Material3 library for consistency with the Compose Material3 library. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I49a0a24345a87de25aba78733c6351ede53c921d">I49a0a</a>)</li>
<li>Wear material and wear material3 components exposing a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> in their API have been updated to now expose a nullable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> that defaults to null. There are no semantic changes here: passing null means that you do not wish to hoist the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, and it will be created inside the component if needed. Changing to null allows for some components to never allocate a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, and allows for other components to only lazily create an instance when they need to, which improves performance across these components. If you are not using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> you pass to these components, it is recommended that you pass null instead. It is also recommended that you make similar changes in your own components.
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib90fc2736d2311e467d7c2a3fef4df757afaf525">Ib90fc</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/298048146">b/298048146</a>)</li>
<li>Adds new ripple API in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear:compose-material</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear:compose-material3</code> libraries which replaces the deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberRipple</code>. Also adds a temporary <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocal</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalUseFallbackRippleImplementation</code>, to revert Material components to using the deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberRipple/RippleTheme</code> APIs. This will be removed in the next stable release, and is only intended to be a temporary migration aid for cases where you are providing a custom <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleTheme</code>. See developer.android.com for migration information and more background information behind this change.
(<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/af92b215fa235f565a4b2e2612f195d67adf9a99">af92b21</a>)</li>
<li>We have made minor improvements to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPageIndicator</code> api and its documentation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I60efcf96f5260a27de394682c5df2ace50e67c93">I60efc</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ColorScheme</code> to be immutable, making individual color updates less efficient, but making more common usage of colors more efficient. The reasoning behind this change is that the majority of apps wouldn&#39;t have updating individual colors as a main use case. This is still possible but it will recompose more than before, in turn we significantly decrease the amount of state subscriptions through all of material code and will impact initialization and runtime cost of more standard use cases. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibc2d6d36f4bdd817c06f686cd1e3c210c2544b82">Ibc2d6</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code> and  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleButton</code> APIs to allow disabled colors to be customized. In addition, Material Design tokens are now used for color and typography values.  (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If087ca889ffa3fce5fac10cc813551838b6cfd03">If087c</a>)</li>
<li>Updated Button image background colors to use Material Design tokens. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iba21513fbc8f65a628cfa600785607db9f952bed">Iba215</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Checkbox</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> components to be display-only, by removing the click handling. These components are expected to be used in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">(Split)ToggleButton</code> which handles the click, so the components are now more clearly indicated as display-only (and are not intended for standalone use on Wear). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2322ed56b42d364dfaa98e7ba72ff62b4fb5b9c3">I2322e</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added tokens for motion values of durations and easings in Wear Compose Material 3. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I437cdff8bf33081b3d0930f4ca1d0631695cbb34">I437cd</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Checkbox</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> so that accessibility announcements are not repeated (previously, semantic roles were duplicated). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ica281335ebabdf52577720e5cda72420adb90cbd">Ica281</a>)</li>
<li>We have removed the materialcore layer for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> to improve performance. (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/7902858b7a46c87a4f24f5da0111ed2a5d244bfc">7902858</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha15" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha15" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha15</h3>

<p>November 15, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha15</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/465c5c5b7a0d79793bddb26a695f67aba8ea2f7e..1f80a6f0c1cb96288c04124001fa2c9bd29617d6/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha15 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have renamed the Foundation level <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code>. This makes the distinction clearer between the Foundation level component and the Material3 level <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>. The latter pulls colors from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code> to be used in scrims and delegates the remaining implementation to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibecfc1720eadd2d8e5e1c1cfd6832300775bffb1">Ibecfc</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>July 26, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha08</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494..4aed940027a19667e67d155563fc5fa8b7279313/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha08 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added the following selection controls for Material3 - <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Checkbox</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib918caf8afcc96b280efc3b99ea31ad7e870522b">Ib918c</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconToggleButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextToggleButton</code> to Material3,  a circular toggle button with a single slot for icon and text respectively.  For different sizes of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code>, we recommend using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.touchTargetAwareSize</code> with the sizes provided in respective toggle buttons. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9f0157a37ca42988afc898eddff84d2b4a048926">I9f015</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListSubheader</code> to our Material3 components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibaefe0204c4afbfd5dfa80565b1cce99cdd47391">Ibaefe</a>)</li>
<li>We have added Material3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>, which calls the new Foundation <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> and supplies default color values from its theme. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I275fbd752435e183fd99594ae16bca5a8c92f864">I275fb</a>)</li>
<li>We have added the Material3 <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> to Wear Compose. It allows users to make a selection from a range of values. The range of selections is shown as a bar between the minimum and maximum values of the range, from which users may select a single value. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> is ideal for adjusting settings such as volume or brightness. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7085f3340fcc76556fadb06ff81c598ae84eacdc">I7085f</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the Shapes in Wear Material 3 theme to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RoundedCornerShape</code> based instead of Shape. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idb133928caec559027d0151d96e86f955edccb4a">Idb133</a>)</li>
<li>We have made the height constants for Button public (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idbfdecfdc391dd2591724d3e6ba9c34f0e20878a">Idbfde</a>)</li>
<li>Updated API files to annotate compatibility suppression (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8e87ae292b38fac1886001f5317acda1592f174b">I8e87a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/287516207">b/287516207</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSliderColors</code> in Wear Compose Material 3 to have  public constructor and public properties. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6b6326d898fc4d96078ecab413e21306c8f7c37d">I6b632</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated all color classes in Wear Compose Material 3 to have public constructors and public properties. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I177024b33ad10c324871c75c25e64ecef480e895">I17702</a>)</li>
<li>We have made Button horizontal and vertical padding constants public. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieeaf7e002e40394df0b591e8ff1e8d92e55a061f">Ieeaf7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Button will now adjust its height to accommodate content that has grown due to  large fonts for accessibility, when required (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaf3026bfb19a261821878927b0e0e3aaacca57c1">Iaf302</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated a number of Button demos to address accessibility issues. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I61ce9c80437224e210d39be789d775163f140ca8">I61ce9</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> now support repeated clicks on long press so that you can quickly increase/decrease value of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> by holding the + or - buttons (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2735993c5721f8a4142b3ca09bca42364da69059">I27359</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha07</h3>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha07</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/df792c9ff86d87f538bab5d7f9dd9f56e2437b15..3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha07 contains these commits.</a></p>

This is similar to the previous Material version, but omits range semantics by default, following developer feedback. We provide <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.rangeSemantics</code> the cases where range semantics are required.
