<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>May 24, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha05</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6f3ac2bd197d5e61ab2708125b57d6ae4003ad68..06ba27a6a7d155acd0b8eea379b0948333901d86/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code> to Material3, a circular button with a single slot for text. For different sizes of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code>, we recommend using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.touchTargetAwareSize</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExtraSmallButtonSize</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SmallButtonSize</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DefaultButtonSize</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LargeButtonSizeIcon</code> provided in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButtonDefaults</code>. The default <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code> has no border and a transparent background for low emphasis actions. For actions that require high emphasis, use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">filledTextButtonColors</code>; for a medium-emphasis, outlined <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextButton</code>, set the border to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonDefaults.outlinedButtonBorder</code>; for a middle ground between outlined and filled, use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">filledTonalTextButtonColors</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I667e4b7c85311f677de8332fc537f84148b18378">I667e4</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Card</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedCard</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AppCard</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TitleCard</code> into the Wear Compose Material3 library. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AppCard</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TitleCard</code> can also be given the outlined appearance using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.outlinedCardColors</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.outlinedCardBorder</code>(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I80e721a921d396fbbf5dc27b4bafd836fc188cb1">I80e72</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have moved the Button label parameter to the end to support trailing lambda syntax and removed the role parameter (as this can be overridden using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.semantics</code>). <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ButtonColors</code> constructors are now public. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie1b6d55ea940e98ab1d41f863587df4b6554433a">Ie1b6d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>May 10, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/01bd392d5702480f8bfe61a8f8bbbea64cf362a0..6f3ac2bd197d5e61ab2708125b57d6ae4003ad68/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code> to Material3, a circular button with a single slot for icon/image. There are four variations: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledIconButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledTonalIconButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedIconButton</code>. For different sizes of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButton</code>, we recommend using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.touchTargetAwareSize</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExtraSmallButtonSize</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SmallButtonSize</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DefaultButtonSize</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LargeButtonSizeIcon</code> provided in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButtonDefaults</code>. We also provide <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IconButtonDefaults.iconSizeFor</code> to determine the recommended icon size for a given button size. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I721d46af2b1d2d17185cbcf530e831f03a53e47e">I721d4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>April 19, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a200cb82769634cecdb118ec4f0bfdf0b086e597..01bd392d5702480f8bfe61a8f8bbbea64cf362a0/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added the Material 3 Button component - this is our stadium-shaped button and was formerly named Chip in the Wear Compose Material library (it has been renamed to Button for consistency with the Compose Material 3 library). The default Button has a filled background and there are button variations for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">FilledTonal</code> (muted background), Outlined (transparent with a thin border) and Child (transparent background and no border, used for supplementary actions with the lowest amount of prominence). Round buttons for simple icon and text content will follow in a future release.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia69423e823d0b307a1b0a4782dcdd58659731c77">Ia6942</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>April 5, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5e7d256f82fbafb6d059ab7b18fddd87c7531553..a200cb82769634cecdb118ec4f0bfdf0b086e597/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DefaultTextStyle</code> to Wear Compose Material 3 which defaults the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextStyle.includeFontPadding</code> to true (the current setting). This will allow us to synchronize turning off font padding by default with the Compose libraries in the future (see <a href="https://medium.com/androiddevelopers/fixing-font-padding-in-compose-text-768cd232425b">Fix font padding in Compose for background</a>). (<a href="https://android-review.git.corp.google.com/q/I7e461cf9492e85077b05a9eb79dc108da1a81015">I7e461</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="material3-1.0.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>March 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3:1.0.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5e7d256f82fbafb6d059ab7b18fddd87c7531553/wear/compose/compose-material3">Version 1.0.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p>Material 3 is the next evolution of Material Design and includes updated theming and redesigned components. Material 3 on Wear Compose is designed to be cohesive with the Material 3 Compose library on Android. This first alpha release contains early, functional implementations of the following:</p>

<ul>
<li>Material theme - configures the color scheme, typography and shapes consistently across components in the library. The Material3 theme has revised colors which support accessible contrast. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8400524e8aaa1d3231571a1e29ba75850cc7f9ab">I84005</a>)</li>
<li>Text/Icon - building blocks for Wear Compose apps (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/2b07cd3007cc2a2afd2e730e46cd584ccafab343">I8e06a</a>)</li>
</ul></li>
<li><p>We will continue to develop Wear Material (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material</code>) and Wear Material 3 (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material3</code>) in parallel. Future material3 releases will extend the widget set to include other familiar components from Compose for Wear OS, such as buttons, pickers, and sliders. </p></li>
<li><p>The Wear Material and Wear Material 3 libraries are mutually exclusive and should not be mixed in the same app, primarily because they reference different themes which would lead to unexpected inconsistencies.</p></li>
</ul>

<h2 id="wear_compose_version_15_2" data-text="Wear Compose Version 1.5" tabindex="-1">Wear Compose Version 1.5</h2>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>December 11, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.5.0-alpha07</code> is released. Version 1.5.0-alpha07 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6f09cf2ae979e48fdb19485f757a033e4a34bb82..46295bc0b75a16f452e8e0090e8de41073d4dbb6/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumnState</code> now provides a way to observe the current scroll progress based on anchor item indices. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I72b0145ee6f41146f2f0a29747f0274c1a7bc729">I72b01</a>)</li>
<li>We have added animations to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> when adding, removing and moving items, if they have the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.animateItem</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iecb9cb2cc65e36ebca3378c459ed1db5f9714ff0">Iecb9c</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> now exposes values for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">beforeContentPadding</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">afterContentPadding</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iccd5f33678875101820e999782e2cc6178feccb0">Iccd5f</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> now provides the composition  local <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalTransformingLazyColumnItemScope</code> which components (such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Card</code>s and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button</code>s in Material3) can use to automatically morph when placed inside a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code>. Callers can disable automatic morphing using the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformExclusion</code> wrapper. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1652f87699096f3de1cef247d714099a105647a2">I1652f</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated min and max fling velocities for rotary on devices targeting U onwards. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I33559a1b3b8c37ebac3f7f363b3323ea14e2cc94">I33559</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a crash that occurred if an item in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> did not contain any composables (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idb99d23985eb1c967930eb2426b1119121f4a0ae">Idb99d</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollFeedbackProvider</code> support for rotary haptics on Android Vanilla ice cream. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibc553fa30c3b061586db76345c341df54491edfb">Ibc553</a>)</li>
<li>We have applied an increased touch slop when using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> in order to reduce the chances of accidentally triggering a swipe when vertically scrolling. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic0672b13fa481c05bff4017065813f89eeb666b7">Ic0672</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PredictiveBackHandler</code> when available with API 35 onwards. In that case,  new animations will be applied. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I08c119056e5ed164a4b0eec73cd5e802f858a3f1">I08c11</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>November 13, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.5.0-alpha06</code> is released. Version 1.5.0-alpha06 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ccd90a76bd7c4acf4f4f01eca76350e383bc441e..6f09cf2ae979e48fdb19485f757a033e4a34bb82/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have simplified the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollInfoProvider</code> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PagerState</code> by removing the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">orientation</code> parameter, which is no longer needed. The new behavior is for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> to remain in place for both horizontal and vertical paging. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I71767df0f68f4109e8ac79aa37a075ff4b3179a3">I71767</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> was introduced in earlier releases. We are now removing Wear&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> aliases (which were forwarding to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code>) in favor of the new name <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code>.  We have also removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumnVisibleItemInfo</code>&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">height</code> property - please use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">measuredHeight</code> instead. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0ea1ed2751443be3001b93d454c4ad9587956541">I0ea1e</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PagerDefaults.snapFlingBehavior</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snapAnimationSpec</code> from a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Tween</code> to a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Spring</code> spec.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I10d0275b7f3b957af279893d2ed52d63e42b8115">I10d02</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/349781047">b/349781047</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/303807950">b/303807950</a>)</li>
<li>We have promoted the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalReduceMotion</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocal</code> to stable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia6f32294df59ee0a6cd74f44784936b024c0af45">Ia6f32</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.rotaryScrollable</code> to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">focusTargetWithSemantics</code> for better semantics support in rotary. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ief0a01182138ba5ce6991a99ccb537e49183d673">Ief0a0</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the minimum API dependency to 1.7.4 for Compose libraries. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I88b4613796d9c9ccccf3f3a1cf0efd3ad6ce2f41">I88b46</a>)</li>
<li>We have disabled width morphing in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> as a workaround to a clipping bug. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3dfb80e56cea3fbc5fb21081cc2f163c3fb85119">I3dfb8</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug that caused disappearing items after overscroll with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id766881e9961d1d0e352dccdb4f62ae91b47a249">Id7668</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyLayoutSemantics</code> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia8f56d3967e363a58e3b688258fa884afaa5a83a">Ia8f56</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>October 30, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.5.0-alpha05</code> is released. Version 1.5.0-alpha05 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/b8a68b0896897fa158508d73a31998a26161d9a7..ccd90a76bd7c4acf4f4f01eca76350e383bc441e/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added support for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateScrollTo</code> on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumnState</code> so that scrolling to an item can be animated. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4097d78d645dfda25116eafc93aba6b2abdff3af">I4097d</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">requestScrollTo</code> on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumnState</code> to defer scrolling to the next measurement. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I20a5e716032d422311e7ca6136a9c771c1f1156e">I20a5e</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentPadding</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3a69c58a810bb927e8c44a4ff02bef36390d80c1">I3a69c</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug in rendering the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> when the content height is shorter than the screen height. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6c3e1df767684c2cd65c5633bd4f1be2827f0522">I6c3e1</a>)</li>
<li>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollInfoProvder</code> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> now correctly tracks the first item. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1e4a34d68f5e3bd317cdf24e89980e18bd7ce705">I1e4a3</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumnState</code> now saves its state (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">anchorItemIndex</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">anchorItemScrollOffset</code>). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3d26540cc282a7ade49204f10bb778ae832abf28">I3d265</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>October 16, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.5.0-alpha04</code> is released. Version 1.5.0-alpha04 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/b6ae8d0a0e8cd803f7b84f30101eda1af4f1d6b6..b8a68b0896897fa158508d73a31998a26161d9a7/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have renamed the Wear Compose Foundation <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> so that the distinction is clearer between this and the Compose Foundation <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0608b1772ce548b97328f4fa888dfd44cb1306ae">I0608b</a>)</li>
<li>Added rotary support for Horizontal/Vertical pagers, enabling users to navigate pagers using rotary input devices. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9770d94d93d745228694c50c58360c66a4b82257">I9770d</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PagerDefaults</code> to make clear that the pager will snap-to-page by default. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iff7d026c30a147ca7a40b372dc99cece2ad30665">Iff7d0</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumnItemScrollProgress</code> is now a value class which should improve the performance. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic399eda25eff59b17ea01c02afed457d8535b6b2">Ic399e</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumn</code> now supports rotary out of the box. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I05206ade1df7139035f100ac77dcf645ccd0be86">I05206</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">TransformingLazyColumnState</code> now supports <code translate="no" dir="ltr">scrollToItem</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I507b3768384e1707d9720959be16ef46989daf49">I507b3</a>)</li>
<li>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@ExperimentalWearFoundationApi</code> from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I34a66f5cf4ef9c49043df7513de7858e58994e2d">I34a66</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>October 2, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.5.0-alpha03</code> is released. Version 1.5.0-alpha03 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/0431b84980e97d6bafdfda7c9038bc4d9529564f..b6ae8d0a0e8cd803f7b84f30101eda1af4f1d6b6/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added support for bi-directional swiping in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code>, for rare cases where the current screen does not support swipe to dismiss. . The default is still to swipe-to-reveal only on right-to-left swipes and it is strongly advised to respect the default behavior to avoid conflict with swipe to dismiss. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifac04be22f302315ff1cd2160a44c24c82f29612">Ifac04</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumnState</code> to override <code translate="no" dir="ltr">canScrollForward</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">canScrollBackward</code> - this now stops scrolling when the first or last item is exactly at the center of the screen. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia77d796c29fcb353779b940c930465ba12126557">Ia77d7</a>)</li>
<li>We have added new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPager</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">VerticalPager</code> components which address common issues, such as focus handling and interacting with system swipe to dismiss that could occur on Wear. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2902b5f63e513ee5882194ed5fabb71752b5d980">I2902b</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> to expose the client&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">key</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentType</code> through <code translate="no" dir="ltr">layoutItems</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1bd9c2864b150c7f9432180af4f12181c9fe1914">I1bd9c</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the curved text animations to be smoother, using paint flags. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I73a1549404b219c99388eb3d1f472a625156c664">I73a15</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the Material Dialog documentation to reflect that <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDismissRequest</code> is not called after show flag is set to false. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifd8d6d17abe8b5316a37b56cf08df4226426a058">Ifd8d6</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug with the vignette animation in the Material Dialog (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I126bf30e2fd2d4ca32c736469bb645d21486c024">I126bf</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>September 18, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.5.0-alpha02</code> is released. Version 1.5.0-alpha02 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/80f82d37cb9b40250ee9eb15d9cbe9e93849355e..0431b84980e97d6bafdfda7c9038bc4d9529564f/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added support for the Wear Compose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> with our <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScreenScaffold</code> (and  added an implementation of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollInfoProvider</code> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumnState</code>). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib8d2946c22fe8279d08b0f8fc9029cdf5b8e0423">Ib8d29</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">viewportSize</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumnLayoutInfo</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4187fae58a65c69b4c07e3ef99fa64ace50e1078">I4187f</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug so that rotary scrolling is now disabled in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> when the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">userScrollEnabled</code> flag is set to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">false</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I490ab6859a0ccd7cd12d26acabb8d8a9eade4086">I490ab</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/360295825">b/360295825</a>)</li>
<li>We have made a bug fix to address unexpected vertical padding on curved text. The curved text height now more closely matches the actual space used by the text. Please note that this is likely to break screenshot tests that involve curved text (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaa6ef3ca880041ece108243dc108f04668d6ac78">Iaa6ef</a>)</li>
<li>We have reverted a bug fix to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Dialog</code> where the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDismissRequest</code> callback was called when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showDialog</code> was set to false, because in some cases this resulted in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDismissRequest</code> being called multiple times. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I64656df176525ed88fd6f6e997d4a85688bfc2ce">I64656</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.5.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.5.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.5.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>September 4, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.5.0-alpha01</code> is released. Version 1.5.0-alpha01 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/cd340f20b7c66762f0fc3710282a91b3e6f94ba9..80f82d37cb9b40250ee9eb15d9cbe9e93849355e/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> into the Wear Compose Foundation library with associated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumnState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumnScope</code> APIs. This serves as the foundation for building customisable scaling and morphing effects with Wear Compose. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib3b22b3f81d18e074b6de37a3e6ba4e2d60cb548">Ib3b22</a>)</li>
<li>We have added an indexed version of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">itemsIndexed</code> into <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumnScope</code> as part of the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib4a57f61568d5e210cfc8e6187adf85719ee4b52">Ib4a57</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> modifiers in order to support scaling and morphing behaviors. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie229a1aa8b3411881367fbe1f0c1ee3a57c39c91">Ie229a</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">HierarchicalFocusCoordinator</code> has been promoted to stable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I31035b5d8619074927cb8d80c61d43dbf725f421">I31035</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for letter spacing to curved text. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3c740555aa285e7663c8ec7cd79b15c785e7d70d">I3c740</a>)</li>
<li>Added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rotationLocked</code> parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout.curvedComposable</code> to stop components being rotated. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I668986bc70f5d46873c43e0ca9755ab71fd296b6">I66898</a>)</li>
<li>The temporary <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalUseFallbackRippleImplementation</code> API from wear material and wear material3 has been removed (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I62282046c22960c7421499aef45fd7f7da45cffa">I62282</a>)</li>
<li>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearDevices.SQUARE</code> from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@WearPreviewDevices</code> multi-preview (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I11c028c3f2d1a7308df4a164ea962a0bfe90f703">I11c02</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> now positions the revealed items on the visible  portion of the screen, this helps when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> is used within a  list, so the items are always interactable and never fall outside the  screen. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I38929341a0c1b40d1015f6f03497a1612c50470e">I38929</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code>  now resets the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">lastActionType</code> to None when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animatedTo</code> has completed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I59b03ea31f1dafa18b1faccdcbce1e50623491e4">I59b03</a>)</li>
<li>Improved the documentation for the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rotationLocked</code> parameter on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedComposable</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifbd57c96ae03b689bc385f032bec7c6c05a2d518">Ifbd57</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed a crash when passing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NaN</code> into <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumnSnapFlingBehavior</code>’s  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performFling</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic13dacc86918a8483e9d0f4f8aa04fe8ad7a059d">Ic13da</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed bug on curved layout size modifier (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0fedfc722a16b04467c04c4f52d6de48da4efd97">I0fedf</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for letter spacing specified in &#39;sp&#39;. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9f6e360c45bfdade1dd5366bb8f040c16475703f">I9f6e3</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in Material2 Dialog where the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDismissRequest</code> callback was not being called when the dialog became invisible (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I64656df176525ed88fd6f6e997d4a85688bfc2ce">I64656</a>)</li>
<li>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutCoordinates.introducesFrameOfReference</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutCoordinates.introducesMotionFrameOfReference</code> to better reflect its purpose. Renamed related function to calculate coordinates based on that flag. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3a3301164ea2c08728b09faed6cf72ae089ead72">I3a330</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="version_14_2" data-text="Version 1.4" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4</h2>

<h3 id="1.4.0" data-text="Version 1.4.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0</h3>

<p>September 4, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0</code> is released. Version 1.4.0 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/cd340f20b7c66762f0fc3710282a91b3e6f94ba9..4298b754aeb9f34e33c951b346a5fb6ee6dd41a1/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.3.0</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Picker</code> now support rotary input by default - it is recommended to remove explicit rotary handling and defer to the default system behavior. If necessary, use the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rotaryScrollableBehavior</code> parameter to configure either scroll or snap behavior - for snap behavior, it is recommended to provide snap behavior and touch scrolling capabilities using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">flingBehavior</code> parameter.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.rotaryScrollable</code> is a new modifier that connects rotary events with scrollable containers, allowing users to scroll using a crown or a rotating bezel on their Wear OS device.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> now provides an entry animation for in-app transitions.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is now shown by default when a screen is first displayed.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Additional changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>For a more complete set of the changes introduced in version 1.3.0, see the <a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/androidx/releases/wear-compose#1.4.0-beta01">beta01 release notes</a>.</li>
</ul>

<p>August 21, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-rc01</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-rc01 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f38af45ab941d981ddb4a0759a4bedc5ade90e00..cd340f20b7c66762f0fc3710282a91b3e6f94ba9/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<li>We have updated the Compose dependencies to 1.7.0-rc01 and pinned Wear Compose Navigation to androidx.lifecycle 2.8.3</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.4.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-beta02</h3>

<p>May 29, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-beta02</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-beta02 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6a69101fd0edc8d02aa316df1f43e0552fd2d7c4..fe555cd2859b125be61b919d63c255741025e9d1/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<h3 id="1.4.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-beta01</h3>

<p>May 14, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-beta01</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-beta01 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/fbd1ac175922f44c69a13545d194066ee428b342..6a69101fd0edc8d02aa316df1f43e0552fd2d7c4/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p>The 1.4-beta01 release of Compose for Wear OS indicates that this release of the library is feature complete and the API is locked (except where marked as experimental). Wear Compose 1.4 includes the following new functionality:</p>

<ul>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.rotaryScrollable</code>, a new modifier that connects rotary events with scrollable containers, allowing users to scroll via a crown or a rotating bezel on their Wear OS device. In addition, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Picker</code> now support rotary input by default. Use the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rotaryScrollableBehavior</code> parameter to configure either scroll or snap behavior. For snap behavior, it is recommended to provide snap via the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">flingBehavior</code> parameter as well for touch scrolling.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> now provides an entry animation for in-app transitions.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is now shown by default when a screen is first displayed.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SelectableChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitSelectableChip</code> have been added as a variation on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> - use this with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> in order to provide selectable semantics instead of toggleable semantics for accessibility</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader</code> now supports height adjustments when contents need extra height to accommodate large font sizes.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug where selectable chips  announced double tap to toggle when already selected. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7ed88da3c5f36e6c7484e43d1b245fa5273620ca">I7ed88</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>May 1, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-alpha08</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha08 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/67004410fdbff19f90caa4cc43965ab21dca1943..fbd1ac175922f44c69a13545d194066ee428b342/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have made the following changes to the new rotary API: renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.rotary</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.rotaryScrollable</code>; renamed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RotaryBehavior</code> interface to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RotaryScrollableBehavior</code> and its function <code translate="no" dir="ltr">handleScrollEvent</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performScroll</code>; renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RotaryScrollableAdapter</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RotaryScrollableLayoutInfoProvider</code> and removed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">scrollableState</code> property. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0c8a6325c2cc2b4d4a8c5ef48fe4204fa91ba969">I0c8a6</a>)</li>
<li>We have made additional changes to the rotary API: renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RotaryScrollableLayoutInfoProvider</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RotarySnapLayoutInfoProvider</code> (because this provider is only needed for rotary with snap); changed the type of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snapOffset</code> parameter in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RotaryScrollableDefaults.snapBehavior snapOffset</code> from Int to Dp. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iddebe5662dc30bf33f1f59b44abccea9b0185e0e">Iddebe</a>)</li>
<li>We have renamed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">clickInteractionSource</code> parameter on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitSelectableChip</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">containerInteractionSource</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia8f84767410c92572b78acdccafb249286c760ec">Ia8f84</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the click callback parameter names for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitSelectableChip</code> - from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onClick</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSelectionClick</code> and from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onBodyClick</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onContainerClick</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I32237caea54f0759c9c4c3cc63056c88a3f26399">I32237</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the horizontal padding for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> to 2dp (was 5dp), in order to fix a bug where the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> (scroll bar) overlaps scrollable content. Please note that this change is expected to break existing screenshots that include the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> due to the change of padding. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5747206005bbc1d83d6882cd03ec5d5846f99626">I57472</a>)</li>
<li>We have improved the documentation for the new rotary API by describing the differences between low-res and hi-res rotary devices. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I63abece7d34e61e08ffdd4d77f7a098adba47e09">I63abe</a>)</li>
<li>We have addressed an out-of-range exception in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> that could be triggered when interpolated alpha values were less than zero. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib75a1d5d64111400fc56dad3ed1a23587f9bfc67">Ib75a1</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/335782510">b/335782510</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>April 17, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-alpha07</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha07 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/02b55f664eba38e42e362e1af3913be1df552d55..67004410fdbff19f90caa4cc43965ab21dca1943/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.rotary</code>, a new modifier that connects rotary events with scrollable containers, allowing users to scroll via a crown or a rotating bezel on their Wear OS device. In addition, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> and Picker now support rotary input by default, with new overloads that include the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rotaryBehavior</code> parameter for specifying the configuration of either scroll or snap. If the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rotaryBehavior</code> parameter is set to snap, then it is recommended to provide snap via the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">flingBehavior</code> parameter as well, for touch scrolling. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2ef6f6e4c804e8f2b53f5553ab4e34ddd8bbd9fe">I2ef6f</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">NestedScroll</code> sources Drag and Fling are being replaced by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">UserInput</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SideEffect</code> to accommodate for the extended definition of these sources that now include animations (Side Effect) and Mouse Wheel and Keyboard (UserInput). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I40579c9b053d6bcf477191b212c7a72876a588b7">I40579</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SelectableChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitSelectableChip</code> to make the distinction clearer between toggle controls such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch/Checkbox</code> and selectable controls such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code>. This replaces the previously added overloads of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip/SplitToggleChip</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">selectionControl</code> parameters. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia0217e0c1c71782921ff3daf02c194a1f05dd6d7">Ia0217</a>)</li>
<li>Updated visibility modifier of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IndeterminateStrokeWidth</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ProgressIndicatorDefaults</code> to public. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5b5a4927c39c6f9db22ba0e582205855587be626">I5b5a4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>March 6, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-alpha04</code> is released. Version 1.4.0-alpha04 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/e1b82c49c59d8e976ce558aba5586f6c61bc9054..638a8d3a474af45f6ad5fdc3d6d1836ea42d1778/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a new overload for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code> that takes a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">selectionControl</code> parameter instead of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">toggleControl</code> parameter. This should be used with the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> control in order to provide selectable semantics instead of toggleable semantics for accessibility (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1d6d99fa8003ef0d9326148dad3ecec5142b6dbb">I1d6d9</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated parameter names for the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">selectionControl</code> overload from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSelected</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSelect</code> for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1a971db9ef5b7cc4c218edc8973d87cfb4602c1c">I1a971</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>February 21, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ca2a8cf8da3a3502fccc593974f8085653e38261..e1b82c49c59d8e976ce558aba5586f6c61bc9054/wear/compose">Version 1.4.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.inspectable</code> wrapper has been deprecated. This API will create more invalidations of your modifier than necessary, so its use is now discouraged. Developers are encouraged to implement the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">inspectableProperties()</code> method on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ModifierNodeElement</code> if they would like to expose modifier properties to tooling. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib323690cdea8d9d4739496b95c6be7909dce7d2f">Ib3236</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a documentation bug for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreview*</code> annotations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id526df9a5fdfefec7864e47bb75584e093cf2e4d">Id526d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>February 7, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/51191bc12f96f233fc08995e1b4e8ff8b88bc7ce..ca2a8cf8da3a3502fccc593974f8085653e38261/wear/compose">Version 1.4.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug in swipe-to-reveal, where it was possible to interact with (and cancel) a committed action on one item by starting to swipe another item.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ide059f6818d86e64e98381931c84c1d069de059b">Ide059</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader</code> to support height adjustments when contents need extra height to accommodate large font sizes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7290ce63e80f480bf67da630013b875aa0005ee2">I7290c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/251166127">b/251166127</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.4.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.4.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.4.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>January 24, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.4.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/51191bc12f96f233fc08995e1b4e8ff8b88bc7ce/wear/compose">Version 1.4.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added entry animation to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> for in-app transitions.(<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/cfeb79aea228f03346b7f837340e3d022c0f29cc">cfeb79a</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is now shown by default when a screen is first displayed. This change was introduced in order to help meet Wear Quality guidelines. Unfortunately, it means that screenshot tests will need to be updated on screens that include <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code>, as the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> would not previously have been displayed. (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/419cef709025753de2d4e2e33d57c8359ce51276">419cef7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a new ripple API in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear:compose-material</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear:compose-material3</code> libraries which replaces the deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberRipple</code>. Also adds a temporary <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocal</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LocalUseFallbackRippleImplementation</code>, to revert Material components to using the deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberRipple/RippleTheme</code> APIs. This will be removed in the next stable release, and is only intended to be a temporary migration aid for cases where you are providing a custom <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RippleTheme</code>. See developer.android.com for migration information and more background information behind this change. (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/af92b215fa235f565a4b2e2612f195d67adf9a99">af92b21</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ColorScheme</code> to be immutable, making individual color updates less efficient, but making more common usage of colors more efficient. The reasoning behind this change is that the majority of apps wouldn&#39;t have updating individual colors as a main use case. This is still possible but it will recompose more than before, in turn we significantly decrease the amount of state subscriptions through all of the material code and will impact initialization and runtime cost of more standard use cases. (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/f5c48b7f84d5e37e89330f41fb4b3444206ebb98">f5c48b7</a>)</li>
<li>Wear material and Wear material3 components exposing a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> in their API have been updated to now expose a nullable <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> that defaults to null. There are no semantic changes here: passing null means that you do not wish to hoist the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, and it will be created inside the component if needed. Changing to null allows for some components to never allocate a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code>, and allows for other components to only lazily create an instance when they need to, which improves performance across these components. If you are not using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MutableInteractionSource</code> you pass to these components, it is recommended that you pass null instead. It is also recommended that you make similar changes in your own components. (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/f8fa920a5a088277028bfa4c186aedb235d253c0">f8fa920</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberExpandableState</code> to save expandable state. This  ensures that data is stored when navigating to another screen and restored when coming back to the original screen. (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/5c800956e76db61e0d7436f99bc8472253067633">5c80095</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ReduceMotion</code> setting to use a lifecycle aware listener. (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/7c6b12215fdea6e50e0b5374f53eb20a7f93d112">7c6b122</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchExplorationStateProvider</code>’s Listener to be lifecycle aware (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/be28b01faa4c1821eb8b5de0bb5583b1681923e5">be28b01</a>)</li>
<li>We have removed the materialcore layer for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> to improve performance (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/25db8e9acd8be3f1bd2634265a8dfadc6683682e">25db8e9</a>)</li>
<li>We have made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code> more robust to NaN offsets to avoid exceptions (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/b983739273a8918d6500319f7376da7e893c2ecc">b983739</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code> to ensure alpha values are within the range <a href="/jetpack/androidx/releases/%5B8eb3892%5D(https:/android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/8eb3892aea8625003a33fc921360d3a5e28c724a)">0,1</a></li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Checkbox</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> so that accessibility announcements are not repeated (previously, semantic roles were duplicated) (<a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/d11eeb781c925eaad0acf5502671830a4da62883">d11eeb7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="version_13_2" data-text="Version 1.3" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3</h2>

<h3 id="1.3.1" data-text="Version 1.3.1" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.1</h3>

<p>April 3, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.1</code> is released. Version 1.3.1 contains <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/95bee6d8e62992e7b34e2e9181f811fbbe8f00c6..54c32e5204dcbb910c449dd1f94298bee2537eb6/wear/compose">these commits</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug in swipe-to-reveal, where it was possible to interact with (and cancel) a committed action on one item by starting to swipe another item. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ide059f6818d86e64e98381931c84c1d069de059b">Ide059</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0" data-text="Version 1.3.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0</h3>

<p>January 24, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/692193fadb173ae728edb0fb3945d5d727129dfb..95bee6d8e62992e7b34e2e9181f811fbbe8f00c6/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.2.0</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>The <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/foundation/SwipeToDismissBoxState"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState</code></a> class, <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/foundation/SwipeToDismissValue"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissValue</code></a> enumeration, and <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/foundation/package-summary#(androidx.compose.ui.Modifier).edgeSwipeToDismiss(androidx.wear.compose.foundation.SwipeToDismissBoxState,androidx.compose.ui.unit.Dp)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.edgeSwipeToDismiss</code></a> extension function are now each part of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.foundation</code> package, instead of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.material</code> package. This updated architecture allows you to implement gesture handling independently from other design considerations. Material Design workflows, such as applying colors from a configured theme, are handled separately.</li>
<li>The <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/material/package-summary#SwipeToRevealCard(kotlin.Function1,androidx.wear.compose.foundation.RevealState,kotlin.Function0,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function1,androidx.wear.compose.material.SwipeToRevealActionColors,androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Shape,kotlin.Function0)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealCard</code></a> and <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/material/package-summary#SwipeToRevealChip(kotlin.Function1,androidx.wear.compose.foundation.RevealState,kotlin.Function0,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function1,androidx.wear.compose.material.SwipeToRevealActionColors,androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Shape,kotlin.Function0)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealChip</code></a> classes help you implement the <a href="https://developer.android.com/design/ui/wear/guides/components/swipe-to-reveal"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">recommended swipe-to-reveal guidance</code></a>. The <a href="https://cs.android.com/androidx/platform/frameworks/support/+/androidx-main:wear/compose/compose-material/samples/src/main/java/androidx/wear/compose/material/samples/SwipeToRevealSample.kt"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealSample</code></a> class demonstrates how to use these components.</li>
<li><p>Our 1.3.0-alpha02 release introduced a change that causes <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/material/package-summary#Chip(kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function0,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function1,androidx.wear.compose.material.ChipColors,kotlin.Boolean,androidx.compose.foundation.interaction.MutableInteractionSource,androidx.compose.foundation.layout.PaddingValues,androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Shape,androidx.wear.compose.material.ChipBorder)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code></a> and <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/material/package-summary#ToggleChip(kotlin.Boolean,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function0,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,kotlin.Function1,kotlin.Function1,androidx.wear.compose.material.ToggleChipColors,kotlin.Boolean,androidx.compose.foundation.interaction.MutableInteractionSource,androidx.compose.foundation.layout.PaddingValues,androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Shape)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code></a> objects to grow in height to better support user-selected font scaling. This can cause some clipping to occur. To fix this issue, the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">large</code> shape for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code> now uses a larger corner radius (26 dp instead of 24 dp). <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> objects use this new corner radius to avoid clipping content on the corners of Chip and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code>.</p>

<ul>
<li>Most <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chips</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChips</code> are unchanged, given their default 52 dp height. However, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> objects that contain multiple lines of primary or secondary label text, or for which the height has been overridden, could cause screenshot tests to break.</li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Additional changes</strong></p>

<p>For a more complete set of the changes introduced in version 1.3.0, see the <a href="#1.3.0-beta01">beta01 release notes</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Recommendations for implementation</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>If your app allows users to pan around the screen&#39;s content, such as in a map-based app, turn off swipe handling by setting <code translate="no" dir="ltr">userSwipeEnabled</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">false</code> in the <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/navigation/package-summary#SwipeDismissableNavHost(androidx.navigation.NavHostController,androidx.navigation.NavGraph,androidx.compose.ui.Modifier,kotlin.Boolean,androidx.wear.compose.navigation.SwipeDismissableNavHostState)"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code></a> composable, and include a button that allows users to go to the previous screen.</li>
<li>To turn off animations for a position indicator during fade-in and position-change animations within a scrolling list, use a <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/animation/core/SnapSpec"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SnapSpec</code></a> object.</li>
<li>While waiting for a media app to load content for playback, show a blank <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/compose/ui/text/Placeholder"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Placeholder</code></a> composable.</li>
<li>To create a collection of expandable items on demand, consider using the experimental <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/kotlin/androidx/wear/compose/foundation/ExpandableStateMapping"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExpandableStateMapping</code></a> class.</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-rc01" data-text="Version 1.3.0-rc01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-rc01</h3>

<p>January 10, 2024</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0-rc01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/b76585a287cbcfdae38c3e16e5acbc6e26e808e2..37d04ed2f8dfcced119779f812301352786bc623/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0-rc01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>
<p>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code> large shape to use a 26dp rounded corner radius and this will now be used by Chip and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code>. This change is needed to support height adjustments when contents need extra height to accommodate large font sizes—otherwise, the existing stadium shape clips some text content.</p>

<figure id = "include-font-padding-true">
  <img src="/static/jetpack/androidx/images/ChipFullRoundedCornerTextClipping.svg"
  width = "50%"
  alt = "Text clipped on corners">
  <figcaption><b>Figure 1</b>: Text clipped on corners.</figcaption>
  </figure>

<figure id = "include-font-padding-false">
  <img src="/static/jetpack/androidx/images/ChipLargeCornerNoTextClipping.svg"
  width = "50%"
  alt = "Text not clipped">
  <figcaption><b>Figure 2</b>: Text not clipped.</figcaption>
  </figure>

<p>This change may cause a breakage in screenshot tests.
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2e6ae57e2c7f47521cf48d518fd9ff67e030f6da">I2e6ae</a>)</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.3.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-beta02</h3>

<p>December 13, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0-beta02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/a8915c4ac4e4bfead52d6b42aaffaa87966ab38b..b76585a287cbcfdae38c3e16e5acbc6e26e808e2/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have restored the intended swipe motion in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code>. This had been altered in a previous release, such that the slide part of the transition occurred while the finger was touching the screen. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id8e765f2b14ece5e4b38a89a61b3fc8707a80e53">Id8e76</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.3.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-beta01</h3>

<p>November 15, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0-beta01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/465c5c5b7a0d79793bddb26a695f67aba8ea2f7e..1f80a6f0c1cb96288c04124001fa2c9bd29617d6/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p>The 1.3-beta01 release of Compose for Wear OS indicates that this release of the library is feature complete and the API is locked (except where marked as experimental). Wear Compose 1.3 includes the following new functionality:</p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissValue</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.edgeSwipeToDismiss</code> have been migrated from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.material</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.foundation</code>, along with the underlying swipe-to-dismiss implementation in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code>. This allows the gesture handling for swipe-to-dismiss to be used independently of Material Design, for example from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.navigation</code>. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.material</code> is still recommended to be used with Material Design, because it pulls colors from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code>, then delegates the remaining implementation to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code>. </li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> now supports a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">userSwipeEnabled</code> parameter so that swipe handling can be turned off for screens where it is not required.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code> has improved focus handling using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HierarchicalFocusCoordinator</code>. </li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> has new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealCard</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealChip</code> composables in Material that follow the recommended UX guidance for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Card</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code>. It also has undo support for the secondary action.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">DefaultTextStyle</code>  now turns off font padding to be consistent across the Android Platform.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code> and  <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> now adjust their height to accommodate content that has grown due to large fonts for accessibility</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> now has individual animation specs for the fade-in, fade-out and position-change animations. For performance reasons, we recommend that fade-in and position-change are turned off when used with scrollable lists.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExpandableStateMapping</code> provides a new way to generate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExpandableStates</code> when they need to be created on demand and not necessarily with a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Composable</code> scope.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Placeholder</code> now allows resetting if the content is no longer in the ready state. Also, the reduce motion setting now applies to the shimmering effect and wipe-off motion on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Placeholder</code>.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Known Issues</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is not initially shown when a screen is first displayed. We intend to make a change in an early 1.4 alpha so that it will be initially shown, but without any animation.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have renamed the Foundation level <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code>. This makes the distinction clearer between the Foundation level component and the Material level <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>. The latter pulls colors from the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code> to be used in scrims and delegates the remaining implementation to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicSwipeToDismissBox</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibecfc1720eadd2d8e5e1c1cfd6832300775bffb1">Ibecfc</a>)</li>
<li>We have marked <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberExpandableStateMapping</code> as experimental and improved the performance of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expandableItem</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5f6bc03b5b0c8b8e4a66f03000a3710c368ebf67">I5f6bc</a>)</li>
<li>We have replaced the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealAction</code> class in the Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> Card and Chip APIs with a slot-based API using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealPrimaryAction</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealSecondaryAction</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToRevealUndoAction</code> composables. Please see sample code for examples on how to use the new API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia89431e240b0602bfe08bceb660ff9ef1137d938">Ia8943</a>)</li>
<li>We have replaced the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> animation flags with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnimationSpec</code> parameters. The individual animations can be disabled by passing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snap</code> as the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AnimationSpec</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6c5232868a3e4fcafde3f066a735ae8df203cb54">I6c523</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug triggered by limited curved text when size is limited (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I50efee190c03dcb4e9abc433602623ae4ba955d7">I50efe</a>)</li>
<li>We have addressed a potential NaN crash related to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedComposable</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I970ebced07b80bb3b51b6d6cd8329207be79902b">I970eb</a>)</li>
<li>We have reverted the removal of the position change highlight animation on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieb4245ffbfde4405f948adc98a79b0c11def424e">Ieb424</a>)</li>
<li>We have removed the material-core layer for material Chip to improve its performance. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If2dcbbc99bbb6394b85b7fc8f3c9d88bdc78ba4a">If2dcb</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>October 18, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0-alpha08</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1f7407d4293384a1b91bc142880e3525048b3443..465c5c5b7a0d79793bddb26a695f67aba8ea2f7e/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0-alpha08 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added individual flags to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> overloads, to control different animations: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showFadeInAnimation</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showFadeOutAnimation</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showPositionAnimation</code>. The previous API has been deprecated and forwards calls to the new one. For performance reasons and for UX consistency, when the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is used with a scrollable list, we recommend switching off <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showFadeInAnimation</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showPositionAnimation</code> flags. If <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is used as a standalone indicator, for example for volume change, then we recommend having all 3 animations turned on. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I44294ccbb47f244dda839b4659a1b2cd962c7aef">I44294</a>)</li>
<li>We have deprecated the Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissValue</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">edgeSwipeToDismiss</code> following the migration of Swipe-to-Dismiss functionality to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear.compose.foundation</code>. Please replace with the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear.compose.foundation</code> equivalents. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iee8c97aeb50a9109d35fc70d41c57fb755dab699">Iee8c9</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the baseline profiles for wear compose foundation, material and navigation libraries. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idb060e09eeb5d708f6bf5c531fe9c01b7e5ae465">Idb060</a>)</li>
<li>We have reverted a behavioral change for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> introduced in a previous CL, such that the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> was animated when a screen was initially displayed.  We intend to make a similar change in an early 1.4 alpha, so that the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is initially displayed, but without any animation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I41843ef10d4ebad839616c8005070f1989b2e940">I41843</a>)</li>
<li>We have addressed some performance issues in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1c6546abc834f718c9d8f11d756262d507590acc">I1c654</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/302399827">b/302399827</a>)</li>
<li>We have optimized performance of the touch exploration state provider default  implementation to rely on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">State&lt;Boolean&gt;</code> rather than  derived state. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieec4de2ea71eefabb5dbac43d61975e4f36cc5df">Ieec4d</a>)</li>
<li>We have set <code translate="no" dir="ltr">systemGestureExclusion</code> rectangles for Android 13 and higher. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib1f4b09be3efedc382213b58d80f02bb21608e7d">Ib1f4b</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>October 4, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0-alpha07</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/91bb8c1f81dcb031bda00fcd8e55f1e890b56f06..1f7407d4293384a1b91bc142880e3525048b3443/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0-alpha07 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added individual flags to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> to control different animations: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showFadeInAnimation</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showFadeOutAnimation</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showPositionAnimation</code>. The previous API has been deprecated and forwards calls to the new one. For performance reasons and for UX consistency, when the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is used with a scrollable list, we recommend switching off <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showFadeInAnimation</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showPositionAnimation</code> flags. If <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is used as a standalone indicator, for example for volume change, then we recommend having all 3 animations turned on. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia2d63d8ea92ca87b09b11d79c7968f0f72460bab">Ia2d63</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have made improvements to the swipe to reveal motion by adding a fade animation to the primary action text, and fading the secondary action/changing the icon scale on full swipe expansion. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib72232be1be3c7711282f663570d8a9fa7432216">Ib7223</a>)</li>
<li>It is recommended that Swipe to Reveal actions are made accessible and we have added custom accessibility actions to our Swipe to Reveal samples. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I422247105b834eec718b76cbb2b3d77e9085d998">I42224</a>)</li>
<li>We have improved the performance of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>, including refactoring to ensure that the initial logic does not trigger a recomposition. The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> is now drawn as the full screen size. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie0aa2d6ef7c2cea5a96d5b268cfd2e0545b402a1">Ie0aa2</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug when the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> incorrectly disappeared. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2091a88014bbaccf5ff6171d9bf2c50c96d4ae36">I2091a</a>)</li>
<li>Improved performance of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> by optimizing recompositions. New flags to control the animations (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">fadeIn</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fadeOut</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">positionChange</code>) have been added subsequently (see API Changes) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifac7de410fc3d68a604cc1212abe19d1de9d6f06">Ifac7d</a>)</li>
<li>We have added Microbenchmark tests for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idf8756cae7809140d50e7de19f60ddedbf8aac03">Idf875</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha03</h3>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/4aed940027a19667e67d155563fc5fa8b7279313..5d7dd999525725bd038a00ca4e89e0fef624a6da/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<ul>

(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7ec65ff3e6c419685f5f3e80a3073ee78143feb0">I7ec65</a>)</li>
