<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>July 26, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494..4aed940027a19667e67d155563fc5fa8b7279313/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have provided <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExpandableStateMapping</code>, a new way to generate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExpandableStates</code>, for cases in which they need to be created on demand, not necessarily within a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Composable</code> scope (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iff9e0dc927754c763ec0c1c0b9760ec5a8f20ef5">Iff9e0</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> has been migrated from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.material</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.foundation</code> package. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I275fbd752435e183fd99594ae16bca5a8c92f864">I275fb</a>)</li>
<li>Updated API files to annotate compatibility suppression. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8e87ae292b38fac1886001f5317acda1592f174b">I8e87a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/287516207">b/287516207</a>)</li>
<li>We have made the height constants for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> public (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idbfdecfdc391dd2591724d3e6ba9c34f0e20878a">Idbfde</a>)</li>
<li>We have made the horizontal and vertical paddings for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactChip</code> public. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieeaf7e002e40394df0b591e8ff1e8d92e55a061f">Ieeaf7</a>)</li>
<li>Added functionality to turn off swipe handling in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> via the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">userSwipeEnabled</code> parameter. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id2a0befd6895598967ccc6d617a7d4b52756b8c6">Id2a0b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/230865655">b/230865655</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the Wear Compose Navigation library to use the new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> from Wear Compose Foundation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4ff8e566a8975d461b97e7a5a3da3435c564390c">I4ff8e</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a z-order bug where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expandedItem</code> did not show the correct content after clicking a button&#39;s behavior when they have buttons. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1899d8055e5ebd89263fc498964565215452e95c">I1899d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/289991514">b/289991514</a>)</li>
<li>Improve focus handling of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> (and hence <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code>) using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HierarchicalFocusCoordinator</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I45362046141d2460c65f392650000c9b86aef6a5">I45362</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/277852486">b/277852486</a>)</li>
<li>We have made a fix to the gesture handling in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeableV2</code> . (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I89737359b27a8dbf21654c2b811b1269f4a27dc6">I89737</a>)</li>
<li>We have finalized the baseline profiles for our 1.2 release. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id57402fffd2612f99e3e36c74891ce1f06dad1ed">Id5740</a>)</li>
<li>Following the migration of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> to Foundation, the Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> implementation now forwards to Foundation and supplies default color values from its theme.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If845146ee4f29d07a950b1bf3b5c9e308e59ab5b">If8451</a>)</li>
<li>We have added heading semantics to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icb25d61b04a3c906f5bc604a5eda803bfb0bc6ff">Ic5420</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> will now adjust their height to accommodate content that has grown due to  large fonts for accessibility, when required. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaf3026bfb19a261821878927b0e0e3aaacca57c1">Iaf302</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed a bug in the semantic role of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code>’s tappable area, for accessibility. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieed3a16f8d534fa39dcea1a3ee4c4641ecef0627">Ieed3a</a>)</li>
<li>The reduce motion setting now turns off the shimmering effect and wipe-off motion on placeholders. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I91046a0ba3a3110a7f041811a630fae8a80c80fd">I91046</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> now support repeated clicks on long press so that you can quickly increase/decrease value of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> by holding the + or - buttons. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2735993c5721f8a4142b3ca09bca42364da69059">I27359</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.3.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.3.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.3.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>June 21, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.3.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/df792c9ff86d87f538bab5d7f9dd9f56e2437b15..3b5b931546a48163444a9eddc533489fcddd7494/wear/compose">Version 1.3.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>As announced in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.2.0-alpha07</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.2.0-alpha10</code>, we are now changing the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DefaultTextStyle</code> to turn off font padding to be consistent across the Android Platform. This will address some cases of text clipping with large font sizes and may also impact screen layouts, so that screenshot tests need to be updated. For example, we see text clipping here (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic6a8606eaa2bb5a360242b61c34c194370521f3b">Ic6a86</a>)</li>
</ul>

<figure id = "include-font-padding-true">
  <img src="/static/jetpack/androidx/images/IncludeFontPadding-True.png"
  width = "50%"
  alt = "Text clipped with large font size">
  <figcaption><b>Figure 1</b>: Text clipped.</figcaption>
  </figure>

<ul>
<li>It is no longer present when font padding is turned off:</li>
</ul>

<figure id = "include-font-padding-false">
  <img src="/static/jetpack/androidx/images/IncludeFontPadding-False.png"
  width = "50%"
  alt = "Text not clipped with large font size">
  <figcaption><b>Figure 2</b>: Text not clipped.</figcaption>
  </figure>

<ul>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear.compose.foundation</code> to be an API dependency of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear.compose.material</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I72004e7a328438e2f0bc8822e0b8e45b5d7225e8">I72004</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/285404743">b/285404743</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>. Background and content keys are now passed to the remember block so that new modifiers are created when the content or background changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib876c266c8ec9795e8f2c83a6c0a7e846b0ebc51">Ib876c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/280392104">b/280392104</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> to use the locale when choosing the format for 12 or 24 hour time. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If4a3d656f72d1e0dd07c1109d457bed75cac8a90">If4a3d</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed an inconsistency in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentScrimColor</code> default parameters. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2d70f70ae0d88f5e744808ac9f40546d2a3b6213">I2d70f</a>)</li>
<li>We have improved the motion handling in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I28fb781b9ff141c7953ca32c7db5f5e663a1a786">I28fb7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Known Issues</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Supporting user-configured font sizes is an accessibility requirement. We know that multiline Chips can lead to text-clipping when displayed with large font sizes, so we will be updating Chip in an early 1.3 alpha version to make height adjustments in those cases. </li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.2.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-beta01</h3>

<p>May 24, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-beta01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6f3ac2bd197d5e61ab2708125b57d6ae4003ad68..06ba27a6a7d155acd0b8eea379b0948333901d86/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>What’s in Compose for Wear OS 1.2</strong></p>

<p>The 1.2-beta01 release of Compose for Wear OS indicates that this release of the library is feature complete and the API is locked (except where marked as experimental). Wear Compose 1.2 includes the following new functionality:</p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">expandableItem</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expandableItems</code> are two new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation</code> components that support expanding items within a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code>. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expandableItem</code> for a single expandable item, such as Text in which the number of lines. Use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expandableItems</code> for a group of expandable items and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">expandableButton</code> to simplify creating a button that collapses after the content is expanded.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">HierarchicalFocusCoordinator</code> - this experimental composable enables marking sub-trees of the composition as focus enabled or focus disabled.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Picker</code> - the API now includes <code translate="no" dir="ltr">userScrollEnabled</code> to control whether the picker is active for user scrolling.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code> - a new composable for handling multiple pickers together. It handles focus between the pickers using the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HierarchicalFocusCoordinator</code> API and enables auto-centering of picker items.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Placeholder</code> - we have made updates to the shimmer and ‘Wipe Off’ animations. The wipe-off effect is now immediately applied when the content is ready.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> - we have migrated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> and associated classes from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.material.ScalingLazyColumn</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.foundation.lazy.ScalingLazyColumn</code>. Please update to use the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation.Lazy</code> version.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code> - we have added experimental support for swipe-to-reveal as a means to access secondary actions, supplementing the existing ‘long press’ pattern.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> - now has an overload with an additional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">enableRangeSemantics</code> parameter to facilitate disabling the default range semantics.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Previews</code> - we have added the following custom annotations for previewing composables on Wear screens: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewSmallRound</code> previews the composable on a small, round device; <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewLargeRound</code> previews the composable on a large round device; <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewSquare</code> previews the composable on a square device. Also, the following and multi-preview annotations: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewFontScales</code> previews the composables on a wear device with multiple font sizes, while <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewDevices</code> previews the composables on different wear devices.</li>
<li>We have added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DefaultTextStyle</code> to Wear Compose which defaults the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextStyle.includeFontPadding</code> property to true (this is the current setting). This will allow us to synchronize turning off font padding by default with the Compose libraries in an early 1.3 alpha version - see <a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/androidx/releases/wear-compose#1.2.0-alpha10">1.2.0-alpha10</a> for more information.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added experimental support for disabled scaling and fading animation when reduce_motion setting is switched on. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5802434d7978c582cddeb5667c26cf7b4fcb9c89">I58024</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Improved documentation for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">angularWidthDp</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedSize.kt</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iab75c401bafba08ce4f2e07ca686b8f5d0685ec3">Iab75c</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> now logs a warning with potential causes of empty backstack. This is done to prevent unexpected crashes caused because of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IllegalArgumentException</code> which was thrown when the backstack was empty. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I04a812325b4a8b5d59d4ce1ba2f770ee75b0ba71">I04a81</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/277700155">b/277700155</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha10" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha10" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha10</h3>

<p>May 10, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-alpha10</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/01bd392d5702480f8bfe61a8f8bbbea64cf362a0..6f3ac2bd197d5e61ab2708125b57d6ae4003ad68/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-alpha10 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added support for Swipe to Reveal, as a means to access secondary actions. This pattern supplements the ‘long press’ pattern, the existing way a user could reveal (different) secondary actions. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I60862f2a9bcb904b0281e3c85b56aaf2a057a976">I60862</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RevealScope</code> to action composables in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToReveal</code>, which gives access to the offset at which additional actions are revealed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3fd56eb7f8f5f9ec467790988afb9f942766098d">I3fd56</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed an issue with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> being stuck on Wear API 33 after fling (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic45992479e12e57ef37625ff923cb7980709b124">Ic4599</a>)</li>
<li>We have made some performance improvements to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> for jank reduction. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I35e9212abd5dfbcfb270442eea7c357db9fc06f5">I35e92</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in Chip and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactChip</code> where the semantic role was no longer being set to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Role.Button</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I93f91a670052b94387349e6ac9e1373353c1e4e2">I93f91</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/277326264">b/277326264</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Known Issues</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p>We have identified a bug in Android Studio which causes failure in rendering preview when annotated with @WearPreviewDevices and @WearPreviewFontScales - a fix is planned for release soon. Please note that the other wear preview annotations work as intended in Android Studio Giraffe 2022.3.1 and beyond.</p></li>
<li><p>In version <a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/androidx/releases/wear-compose#1.2.0-alpha07">1.2.0-alpha07</a> we added DefaultTextStyle to Wear Compose, maintaining the existing PlatformTextStyle.includeFontPadding value as true - for background, see <a href="https://medium.com/androiddevelopers/fixing-font-padding-in-compose-text-768cd232425b">Fix font padding in Compose</a>. We will be changing the DefaultTextStyle to turn off font padding in an early 1.3 alpha version, to be consistent across the Android Platform. This will address some cases of text clipping with large font sizes and may also impact screen layouts, so that screenshot tests need updating. For example, with large font sizes we see text clipping here:</p></li>
</ul>

<figure id = "include-font-padding-true">
  <img src="/static/jetpack/androidx/images/IncludeFontPadding-True.png"
  width = "50%"
  alt = "Text clipped with large font size">
  <figcaption><b>Figure 1</b>: Text clipped.</figcaption>
  </figure>

<ul>
<li>It is no longer present when font padding is turned off:</li>
</ul>

<figure id = "include-font-padding-false">
  <img src="/static/jetpack/androidx/images/IncludeFontPadding-False.png"
  width = "50%"
  alt = "Text not clipped with large font size">
  <figcaption><b>Figure 2</b>: Text not clipped.</figcaption>
  </figure>

<p>The new setting can be adopted now by overriding the typography in your theme - see <a href="https://gist.github.com/shumelchyk/8450933e176cd9044ead7bb38923a3b6">example code</a>.</p>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>March 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-alpha07</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3f3da5079e3673cd35c9f14ffb59b9d21d6fd1b6..5e7d256f82fbafb6d059ab7b18fddd87c7531553/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-alpha07 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have moved the Expandable Item components (added in 1.2.0-alpha06) from material to foundation, since they had no meaningful reference to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib052565ab33d190655b6fae6e7a2e44f743313dd">Ib0525</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a crash that occurred in a screen using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code>, by ensuring that <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code> handles focus correctly when no Picker has the focus. Also added support for RSB scrolling in our Picker demos. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If8c19c69617d2cad60d8e1897bafa55b632c735e">If8c19</a>)</li>
<li>We have improved the dialog transitions - the intro transition is now smoother to match the outro transition. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib5af9b7c468543e8fb5988b50bf712bbfb1a340f">Ib5af9</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DefaultTextStyle</code> to Wear Compose which defaults the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlatformTextStyle.includeFontPadding</code> property to true (this is the current setting). This will allows us to synchronize turning off font padding by default with the Compose libraries in the future - see (<a href="https://medium.com/androiddevelopers/fixing-font-padding-in-compose-text-768cd232425b">Fix font padding in Compose</a>) for background. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2aee81620b17057aab192c02e888392f3c0c96f6">I2aee8</a>)</li>
<li>Reverted an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">UpsideDownCake</code> preview dependency via activity-compose that blocked publishing apps to the Google Play Store. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6443d4e7b9b568ad4d7e19d966c23e66e863ddce">I6443d</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>March 8, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-alpha06</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/3f3da5079e3673cd35c9f14ffb59b9d21d6fd1b6/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-alpha06 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedBox</code> component, which places components on top of each other in the curved world. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I29200406c7f7ea37d750ffcd8f478d3c8b2ea7b8">I29200</a>)</li>
<li>Added Expandable Item(s) - two new components to support either a group of expandable items in a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code>, or an expandable single item, such as Text in which the number of lines expands. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I95dd5f8d5e1d76ee6cb08b176b109d74c0c543ef">I95dd5</a>)</li>
<li>We have added the following custom annotations for previewing composables on Wear screens: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewSmallRound</code> previews the composable on a small, round device; <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewLargeRound</code> previews the composable on a large round device; <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewSquare</code> previews the composable on a square device. Also, the following and multi-preview annotations: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewFontScales</code> previews the composables on a wear device with multiple font sizes, while <code translate="no" dir="ltr">WearPreviewDevices</code> previews the composables on different wear devices. To use these previews, you must be using the latest Android Studio   (Giraffe Canary 6) or beyond. Please note that if these annotations do not suit your purpose, Preview can still be used and supports further customisations via parameters. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I397fff28367e369c2d6870d9e0da3f068ca67e60">I397ff</a>)</li>
<li>We have marked <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HierarchicalFocusCoordinator</code> as experimental while it is considered as a candidate to be moved into core compose libraries, given its wide applicability. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3a768ff9eb2f1cbd46e6ac73cba89561847611e9">I3a768</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed a bug on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HierarchicalFocusCoordinator</code>, when the lambda  passed in for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">focusEnabled</code> parameter is changed, we now correctly use the new one. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icb3539c74d078f1cfdff7997a0a60ccf481cbbfd">Icb353</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the default disabled content color to Background when using primary colors as the background in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code>. This improves the contrast for accessibility. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I527cc9200d88cf6ab090620f43d7de1b180189cb">I527cc</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>February 22, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-alpha05</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f7337eab774a6ce3b17367d5f31708564b66e677..87533b4ff06971ed59028936cd9b6da988cd4522/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code> API to allow propagating the min constraints to the composable optionally. When set as true, the minimum constraints passed from the parent composable will be allowed on the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code>. If set as false, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code> will reset the minimum constraints. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3e046ae05db206b34b106c5601891de0e3913e0a">I3e046</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animateScrollToOption</code> to the Picker API in order to support programmatic animation to a specific Picker option (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6fe679e1c9d168f1da542467ee8041a6ac0a7586">I6fe67</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPageIndicator</code> to support right-to-left layouts. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia4359e82ffcb7f74512888c4b1e53bd913b9e41e">Ia4359</a>)</li>
<li>Added Screenshot tests for right-to-left layout in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPageIndicator</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6fbb8de0c7b628f665340a1175bcb59c484b559a">I6fbb8</a>)</li>
<li>Added further tests to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHostTest</code> that use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TestNavHostController</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I61d54a8a3a67fb6c1984bdbb3b19af5fa506b427">I61d54</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>February 8, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-alpha04</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/e5dad1e7d1c225f89f7c2d5a39a7a0de8d637d7b..f7337eab774a6ce3b17367d5f31708564b66e677/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code> for handling multiple pickers together using the focus API. It handles the focus between the different pickers, enables auto-centering of the pickers based on parameters and allows developers to change the focus between different pickers while handling the events from the group. In talkback mode, the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerGroup</code> handles the talkback focus by moving the focus to the selected Picker from the group. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6084092455aabe1b0ae58761d11f72bca6991301">I60840</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added an overload to Stepper with an additional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">enableRangeSemantics</code> parameter in order to facilitate disabling the default range semantics (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia61d4b410ac398d253a6debe62bf8c8f01f6565b">Ia61d4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Allow <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> to be nested within a horizontally scrolling page (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iec3f8cd60ec3af87abdb81d12ade6e0b6b005aca">Iec3f8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/266555016">b/266555016</a>)</li>
<li>Improvement of Stepper kdocs and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">StepperTest</code> tests clean-up. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic118ef60d6b9c44b769acc33b055f56cc41ace0e">Ic118e</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.navigation</code> dependency to version 2.5.3 (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If58ed04fd5144c0307d195db1986ec2d37888157">If58ed</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>January 25, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-alpha03</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/adf1c279a86ab3886e1666c08e2c3efba783367b..e5dad1e7d1c225f89f7c2d5a39a7a0de8d637d7b/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have migrated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> (and associated classes) from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.material.ScalingLazyColumn</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">andrdoidx.wear.compose.foundation.lazy.ScalingLazyColumn</code> (see <a href="https://github.com/android/wear-os-samples/issues/663">this example</a> for migration). This new location more closely matches that of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">compose.foundation.lazy.LazyColumn</code> and is more natural as it is not an opinionated Material component. The change is happening now in preparation for a new Material3 library, which we will be working on in parallel with the existing Material library. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I060e778102ae01b859b0642efd7039b2ed69fd69">I060e7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p>The following changes are part of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> migration from Material to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation.Lazy</code>:</p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> apis targeting Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> have been deprecated - please update to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation.Lazy ScalingLazyColumn</code>. Additionally <code translate="no" dir="ltr">anchorType</code> field was added to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListLayoutInfo</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I29d95f1dcb1997a445b5cdb04fe5dd7cd81527d0">I29d95</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> has been marked as deprecated in the Wear Compose Material package (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I16d3409dce206c78db9da178d7e736a212544689">I16d34</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollAway</code> modifier to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState</code> from Wear Compose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation.Lazy</code> and deprecated the overload that took <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState</code> from Wear Compose Material. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifc42c9c35e468b757fd840cfa43df353907b362e">Ifc42c</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the Dialog APIs to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState</code> from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation.Lazy</code> and deprecated the overloads that used Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic896024a00faf50c35ff2addae61339ada11904b">Ic8960</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the Picker APIs to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingParams</code> from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation.Lazy</code> and deprecated the overloads that used Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingParams</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idc3d84c55d88489e3adae02a1c197947810c468b">Idc3d8</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug that caused unnecessary recompositions in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState.centerItemIndex</code> by ensuring that it only pushes updates when the value actually changes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia9f38b1cbd96eac0598fc3c482f73326b86f06b9">Ia9f38</a>)</li>
<li>We have improved the performance of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3933b64e8b94a5008a37fd1f26315ed4d8df2eb5">I3933b</a>)</li>
<li>Added benchmark tests for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> in Wear Compose Foundation (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie00f99910775b6d924bdb73b9917f6bb703937a1">Ie00f9</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated some internal <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> classes methods in Material to use their equivalents from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation.Lazy</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I38aab976a9901b6e28a8b4f0d67e332962b6644e">I38aab</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed some issues in Picker tests and add more tests for checking scroll with offset (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6ac34226d3bcd0f7dbbf12818ac27b0dbf73082c">I6ac34</a>)</li>
<li>We migrated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> Integration Demos to depend on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Foundation.Lazy</code> instead of Material <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic6caa03b0fd887bdfb3c5f4dd5a4eb6d22027db1">Ic6caa</a>)</li>
<li>We have added optional <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fromDate/toDate</code> parameters to our <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> demo (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I961cd2cf102f8b9537e3923dd646f3db19c3649c">I961cd</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>January 11, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-alpha02</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/4a2f5e696614339c1ac21f706c1a17c0285780e7..adf1c279a86ab3886e1666c08e2c3efba783367b/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Android Compose UI tests will now run layout passes for each frame when executing frames to get to idle (e.g. via <code translate="no" dir="ltr">waitForIdle</code>). This may affect tests that assert on individual frames of layout animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8ea08728a395665f9ec7965579797e537b2c35e5">I8ea08</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/222093277">b/222093277</a>)</li>
<li>The parameter <code translate="no" dir="ltr">minLines</code> is added to Wear Text for consistent behaviour with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">BasicText</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I24874b28ff5ee0fab36bbcc052560c8590e6e1bb">I24874</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactChipTapTargetPadding</code> has been made public so that it appears in the documentation (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If1e709a1c1a1252f54d11907cc2e412fd2818db9">If1e70</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/234119038">b/234119038</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Disable multiplatform builds for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">wear.compose</code> packages (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iad3d746b9ac10e554fc796f7c3d7808da509d945">Iad3d7</a>)</li>
<li>Fix kdocs for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">scrollToOption</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6f9a0166eae7c64f31ea3839cac180decfdd62b3">I6f9a0</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderState.rememberPlaceholderState()</code> updated to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberUpdatedState</code> to that the state will update if the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onContentReady</code> lambda. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I02635c21c723a91aa2f5915fe79468a463fd1698">I02635</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/260343754">b/260343754</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a text jittering issue seen in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Picker</code> component by leveraging the new compositing strategy added to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.graphicsLayer</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I993029ef37f128cbb568d4a9b80b8bf8f3534882">I99302</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug that caused flickering in our <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code> demo (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/I660bde5d84f6194ce13011117a3cf2102b2ed152">I660bd</a>)</li>
<li>We have improved the accessibility for the 12-hour time and date picker demos (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/I05e12f957e9e386fed9263f103e6ecb2de49c229">I05e12</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated our time and date picker demos so that the pickers are not affected by RSB changes when unselected (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/I4aecb52deb69d14d2327d148d1518d92fed67902">I4aecb</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.2.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.2.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.2.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>December 7, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-*:1.2.0-alpha01</code> is released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/4a2f5e696614339c1ac21f706c1a17c0285780e7/wear/compose">Version 1.2.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We’ve updated the experimental Placeholder functionality so that the “Wipe Off” effect is immediately applied when the content is ready rather than waiting for the next animation loop to start. We have also made some updates to the shimmer and wipe off animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5a7f45c0ce6f2262716de3c2c8131de663910d7b">I5a7f4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HierarchicalFocusCoordinator</code>composable to enable marking sub-trees of the composition as focus enabled or focus disabled.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I827cb73ace07280bb0ad8677755efdf721c46147">I827cb</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a new property to override the semantic role for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code>.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I67132c8ae30e1db80864350ce7a8a3edfb5f8e0d">I67132</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeTextDefaults.TimeFormat12Hours</code> to remove AM/PM in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code>. This will change the default value of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">timeSource</code> parameters in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1eb7fa96f7667217e68b44a3f7cf74d36c24075c">I1eb7f</a>)</li>
<li>We have extended the Picker API to improve accessibility for screens with multi-picker. There is a new property <code translate="no" dir="ltr">userScrollEnabled</code> to control whether the picker is active for user scrolling. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3c3aa55ce84d0d577f3f7ab53a23be915abbc5a1">I3c3aa</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have changed the default border width for an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedButton/OutlinedCompactButton</code> from 2.dp to 1.dp to match final UX specs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icf84ddb21ab10a8b009632e8e71f428578a70c45">Icf84d</a>)</li>
<li>In order to reduce the effect of the first item added to an empty <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> appearing to scroll into place we have added an estimated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">autoCentering topPadding</code> when the contents are empty. This change calculates the amount of top padding needed by assuming an initial item of height 0.dp. For <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListAnchorType.ItemStart</code> this will calculate the correct top padding, for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListAnchorType.ItemCenter</code> this calculation will be incorrect as the height of the items is needed to correctly size the contents resulting in a small scroll into place effect based on the items real height.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I239a415ab2e2427c94d4c23ee74711095b53c309">I239a4</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the background scrim applied to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismiss</code> animation to match the Wear platform. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9003e7d6989497f11983b181378f73d998ffeeb6">I9003e</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> handling of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyListState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState</code> for list items of size 0 to avoid divide by zero errors.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic28dd4452db5b6e0a5e64c3eef48a34641df22cf">Ic28dd</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="version_11_2" data-text="Version 1.1" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1</h2>

<h3 id="1.1.2" data-text="Version 1.1.2" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.2</h3>

<p>February 8, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.2</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.2</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.2</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/ab40086b4e9554c4ddbe6f63ad1bce2ce5b777ae..e632c82e764739f3c9b3696e2b936891c0e11442/wear/compose">Version 1.1.2 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have fixed a bug that caused unnecessary recompositions in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState.centerItemIndex</code> by ensuring that it only pushes updates when the value actually changes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/Ia9f38b1cbd96eac0598fc3c482f73326b86f06b9">Ia9f38</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.1" data-text="Version 1.1.1" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.1</h3>

<p>January 11, 2023</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.1</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.1</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.1</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/079ef6d6d5921bd986bc5a39c018d4cc92d0c07c..ab40086b4e9554c4ddbe6f63ad1bce2ce5b777ae/wear/compose">Version 1.1.1 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">PlaceholderState.rememberPlaceholderState()</code> updated to use <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberUpdatedState</code> to that the state will update if the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onContentReady</code> lambda. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I02635c21c723a91aa2f5915fe79468a463fd1698">I02635</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/260343754">b/260343754</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0" data-text="Version 1.1.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0</h3>

<p>December 7, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f76465e42639496c7a831c4d88e4588b7440bec2..079ef6d6d5921bd986bc5a39c018d4cc92d0c07c/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Important changes since 1.0.0</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Stable release of Compose for Wear OS 1.1.0 (<a href="https://android-developers.googleblog.com/2022/12/compose-for-wear-os-11-stable.html">read more</a>).</li>
<li>For a list of the key changes in Wear Compose 1.1 see the release notes for (<a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/androidx/releases/wear-compose#1.1.0-beta01">Compose for Wear OS 1.1 Beta01</a>).</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We’ve updated the experimental Placeholder functionality so that the “Wipe Off” effect is immediately applied when the content is ready rather than waiting for the next animation loop to start. We have also made some updates to the shimmer and wipe off animations. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5a7f45c0ce6f2262716de3c2c8131de663910d7b">I5a7f4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have changed the default border width for an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedButton/OutlinedCompactButton</code> from 2.dp to 1.dp to match final UX specs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icf84ddb21ab10a8b009632e8e71f428578a70c45">Icf84d</a>)</li>
<li>In order to reduce the effect of the first item added to an empty <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> appearing to scroll into place we have added an estimated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">autoCentering topPadding</code> when the contents are empty. This change calculates the amount of top padding needed by assuming an initial item of height 0.dp. For <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListAnchorType.ItemStart</code> this will calculate the correct top padding, for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListAnchorType.ItemCenter</code> this calculation will be incorrect as the height of the items is needed to correctly size the contents resulting in a small scroll into place effect based on the items real height.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I239a415ab2e2427c94d4c23ee74711095b53c309">I239a4</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the background scrim applied to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismiss</code> animation to match the Wear platform.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9003e7d6989497f11983b181378f73d998ffeeb6">I9003e</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> handling of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyListState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState</code> for list items of size 0 to avoid divide by zero errors.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic28dd4452db5b6e0a5e64c3eef48a34641df22cf">Ic28dd</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-rc01" data-text="Version 1.1.0-rc01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-rc01</h3>

<p>November 9, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-rc01</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-rc01</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-rc01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/548c8ac2570ae6cf15798fea1380491f7d93796b..f76465e42639496c7a831c4d88e4588b7440bec2/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-rc01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added baseline profile rules for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Placeholders</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollAway</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Checkbox</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedCompactButton</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedCompactChip</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8249c85c475cd5e9556be91f5461aea8e4b6d12b">I8249c</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.scrollAway</code> so that if the specified <code translate="no" dir="ltr">itemIndex</code> is invalid (for example, if that item index is out of range), then the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> will now still be displayed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2137a92f7ff86380b8a438708f10cfb678ba8352">I2137a</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> animation to match the platform implementation.  After the initial squeeze animation, the screen now slides off to the right once the dismissal has been triggered. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/I41d34964b0c93d1fef4d188fce749b0f1f0a0474">I41d34</a>)</li>
<li>As an optimization, we have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.scrollAway</code> to only read the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">scrollState</code> inside the measure block to avoid recomposing the modifier after each remeasure. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4c6f17238ee294d98dc56b86153333d7fd5a1aa4">I4c6f1</a>)</li>
<li>We have added documentation and a sample to placeholders to show the correct ordering for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.placeholder</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.placeholderShimmer</code> when applied to the same composable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie96f47734d5ffe91cfbd1f92e1b67543534be41f">Ie96f4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/256583229">b/256583229</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the default border width for an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedCompactChip/OutlinedChip</code> from 2.dp to 1.dp to match final UX specs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib3d8e51de7706b22f592b218fbc454e4b7b4f7a1">Ib3d8e</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberPickerState</code> where updated inputs were not saved, so that composables were not updated after changes to the inputs. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I49ff67e95da966aecbdc3d9b9cdd93bec9f662ba">I49ff6</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/255323197">b/255323197</a>)</li>
<li>We have made some UI updates to the placeholders, 1) change the shimmer gradient to 1.5x the screen size, 2) add easing (cubic bezier) of the shimmer progression and 3) speed up the wipe-off animation (250ms). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id29c1618ef0e680757adc20ba09e483859e56c00">Id29c1</a>)</li>
<li>We have corrected a UI bug in the placeholder wipeOff effect where Chip and Card backgrounds were wiping off slightly early due to not taking the component’s position on screen into account. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2c7cb2ed5d27ec425cca21dca7bf74cab3d3d854">I2c7cb</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the placeholder background drawing to merge colors rather than layer them where possible to reduce the risk of alpha blending of the different cropped layers from allowing underlying colors to bleed through at the placeholder background edges. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2ea2612412ca1fb3cad61c98cfee71ce85bee99f">I2ea26</a>)</li>
<li>We have corrected the calculation of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState.centerItemIndex/centerItemOffset</code> so that if two items sit either side of the viewport center line the one that is closest will be considered as the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">centerItem</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I307091167e04914d1ae29d5324f84ec18ed7b8a8">I30709</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/254257769">b/254257769</a>)</li>
<li>We have corrected a bug in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState.layoutInfo.visibleItemsInfo</code> which was reporting incorrect offsets during <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> initialization. Now an empty list will be returned until all list items are visible and have the correct offsets. Check for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState.layoutInfo.visibleItemsInfo.isNotEmpty()</code> will confirm that the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> initialization is complete and items are visible. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3a3b883d3347784a013b655a0a1e8312d0914ba2">I3a3b8</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.1.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-beta01</h3>

<p>October 24, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-beta01</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-beta01</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-beta01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/4586cf6e518f0c59410ef2b291e34ff9fdcff4e1..548c8ac2570ae6cf15798fea1380491f7d93796b/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>What’s in Compose for Wear OS 1.1</strong></p>

<p>The 1.1.0-beta01 of Compose for Wear OS indicated that this release of the library is feature complete and the API locked.</p>

<ul>
<li>Wear Compose 1.1 release includes the following new functionality:
<ul>
<li>Picker - Accessibility improvements to Picker so that multi-picker screens are navigable with screen readers and the content description is accessible</li>
<li>Picker <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentDescription</code> parameter is now used only for the selected Picker option and takes a nullable String (in the previous commit, it was necessary to pass a mapping from option to the content description, but only the selected option was used).</li>
<li>Picker items are now always center-aligned, fixing a bug when setting <code translate="no" dir="ltr">gradientRatio</code> to zero had the side-effect of changing the alignment.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/ToggleChip</code> -  We have updated the default gradients for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/ToggleChip</code> to bring them in line with the latest UX spec. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ChipDefaults.gradientBackgroundChipColors</code> has been updated to start from 50% of primary rather than 32.5%.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/ToggleChip</code> - Added overloads for modifying Chip shapes</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/Button/ToggleButton</code> - Added a new outlined style for Chips and Buttons and new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedButton</code> composables that provide a transparent <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/Button</code> with a thin border.</li>
<li>Card - Updated the default gradients for Cards to bring them in line with the latest UX spec. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.cardBackgroundPainter</code> has been updated to start from 30% of primary and end at 20% of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSurfaceVariant</code> (was previously 20% to 10% <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSurfaceVariant</code>). <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip.toggleChipColors</code> changes from a linear gradient of 75% surface to 32.5% primary to 0% surface to 50% primary.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button/ToggleButton</code> - Added properties for modifying button shapes.</li>
<li>Theme - Updated a number of the default colors in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code> in order to improve accessibility as the original colors did not have sufficient contrast resulting in difficulties for users to differentiate chip/card/button backgrounds from the theme background color.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider/Stepper</code> - Button roles added so that <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Talkback</code> can recognise them as buttons.</li>
<li>Scaffold - <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> now is positioned and sized so that it only takes the space needed. This is useful, for example, if semantic information is added to it, talkback now gets the correct bounds of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> on screen.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedText/TimeText</code> - Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.scrollAway</code>, which scrolls an item vertically in/out of view, based on scroll state (with overloads to work with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Column</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code>). <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollAway</code> is typically used to scroll a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> out of view as the user starts to scroll a list of items upwards.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedText/TimeText</code> - Added support for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontFamily</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontStyle</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontSynthesis</code> in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedTextStyle</code>, usable on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedText</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">basicCurvedText</code></li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedText/TimeText</code> - Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontWeight</code> to the constructor and copy method on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedTextStyle</code></li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleControls</code> - Added animated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Checkbox</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> toggle controls for use with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code>. These can be used instead of the static icons provided by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChipDefaults</code> (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">switchIcon</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">checkboxIcon</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">radioIcon</code>).</li>
<li>Placeholder - Added experimental placeholder support. This has three distinct visual effects designed to work together.</li>
<li>Firstly a placeholder background brush effect used in containers such as Chip and Cards to draw over the normal background when waiting for content to load.</li>
<li>Secondly a modifier (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.placeholder()</code>) to draw a stadium shaped placeholder widget over the top of content that is being loaded.</li>
<li>Thirdly a modifier gradient/shimmer effect (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.placeholderShimmer()</code>) that is drawn over the top of the other effects to indicate to users that we are waiting for data to load.
<ul>
<li>All of these effects are designed to be coordinated and shimmer and wipe-off in an orchestrated fashion.</li>
</ul></li>
</ul></li>
<li>Core Compose dependencies updated from 1.2 to 1.3</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Font parameters (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontFamily</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontWeight</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontStyle</code> &amp; <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontSynthesis</code>) can now be specified directly as parameters of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedText</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idc422f7433ab3e5bd286a64eb6fcb0f52bece700">Idc422</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">curveText</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">basicCurvedText</code> will now work properly with talkback (the have a properly sized  and placed (but empty) compose-ui node associated with them, using the text as content description) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7af7ced923180839eee782fe2e45a1976c7e8ab4">I7af7c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/210721259">b/210721259</a>)</li>
<li>Bug fix to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Picker</code> when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerState.repeatedItems = false</code> to add an explicit setting of autoCentering params on the Pickers  internal <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> to ensure that it is possible to scroll the zero&#39;th option to the center of the view. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q//I8a4d7e2b018b8be0f5a3e74ce19c44c8fafde91e">I8a4d7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>October 5, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-alpha07</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-alpha07</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-alpha07</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/bdce26bd7556b92d2d4d2af3de881dd8e2c51459..4586cf6e518f0c59410ef2b291e34ff9fdcff4e1/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-alpha07 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added experimental placeholder support. This has three distinct visual effects designed to work together. Firstly a placeholder background brush effect used in containers such as Chip and Cards to draw over the normal background when waiting for content to load. Secondly a modifier (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.placeholder()</code>) to draw a stadium shaped placeholder widget over the top of content that is being loaded. Thirdly a modifier gradient/shimmer effect (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.placeholderShimmer()</code>) that is drawn over the top of the other effects to indicate to users that we are waiting for data to load. All of these effects are designed to be coordinated and shimmer and wipe-off in an orchestrated fashion. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3c33961fa8bdda098b9a992896d49550185e2b86">I3c339</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added support for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontWeight</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontFamily</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontStyle</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontSynthesis</code> in
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedTextStyle</code>, usable on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedText</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">basicCurvedText</code>. Those parameter can be used to specify the font and style to use on the curved text.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaa1a817c1763cc3adc0baf4fcebedeb9578ff440">Iaa1a8</a>),(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I727597b13d3c8bf687076aaae47e03420ef0a8d1">I72759</a>)</li>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.scrollAway</code>&#39;s offset parameter to Dp for consistency with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.offset</code> (previously it was in pixels). Also, refactored as a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutModifier</code> for efficiency. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9f94b1f482dc787dc12858dc3deab3d6b7ba805a">I9f94b</a>)</li>
<li>As part of the new toggle controls API, we have renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton’s circleColor</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ringColor</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I28fa9d0eb30725394d3ec3f7de572ef6d66e7da7">I28fa9</a>)</li>
<li>We have added animated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Checkbox</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Switch</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioButton</code> toggle controls for use with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code>. These can be used instead of the static icons provided by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChipDefaults</code> (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">switchIcon</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">checkboxIcon</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">radioIcon</code>). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8a8c495030cd9186bc583a1670db20a8af8db966">I8a8c4</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>September 21, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-alpha06</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-alpha06</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-alpha06</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/cce7b70f6a5ebf955cf748a73c18b63228b22c74..bdce26bd7556b92d2d4d2af3de881dd8e2c51459/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-alpha06 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.scrollAway</code>, which scrolls an item vertically in/out of view, based on scroll state (with overloads to work with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Column</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code>). <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollAway</code> is typically used to scroll a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> out of view as the user starts to scroll a list of items upwards. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I61766c2fa771df19a0accbd61b04cd22f6ecd7a2">I61766</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> now is positioned and sized so that it only takes the space needed. This is useful, for example, if semantic information is added to it, talkback now gets the correct bounds of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> on screen. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie61067217e778ed0dde816a348e5e116a456d553">Ie6106</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/244409133">b/244409133</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>September 7, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-alpha05</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-alpha05</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-alpha05</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d9910e143f859716fd850a1f0036147622d6089b..cce7b70f6a5ebf955cf748a73c18b63228b22c74/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Button roles were added to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> so that Talkback can recognise them as buttons. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icb46c83b0362d78abc7bc8ec68b9f8938cefb389">Icb46c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/244260275">b/244260275</a>)</li>
<li>We have corrected the z-order of position and page indicators in the Scaffold. The indicators will now sit on top of the vignette and so will not be obscured by the vignette if it is present. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib988f8f73d99fc2cfe5d29d0ea0198e68c391a18">Ib988f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/244207528">b/244207528</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>August 24, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-alpha04</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-alpha04</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-alpha04</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/bea814b246f89ff7244e3c6b0648f0b57e47897c..d9910e143f859716fd850a1f0036147622d6089b/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated a number of the default colors in the MaterialTheme in order to improve accessibility as the original colors did not have sufficient contrast resulting in difficulties for users to differentiate chip/card/button backgrounds from the theme background color. The updated colors are surface(0xFF202124-&gt;0xFF303133), onPrimary(0xFF202124-&gt;0xFF303133), onSecondary(0xFF202124-&gt;0xFF303133), primaryVariant(0xFF669DF6-&gt;0xFF8AB4F8) and onError(0xFF202124-&gt;0xFF000000). The changes in colors though relatively subtle may impact existing screenshot tests.
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/81ab090f2e057a2810618a9d2a2f57c11c454d0c">81ab09</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fix a logic bug in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> that could result in lists with  a small (typically exactly 2) number of list items not completing initialization and as a result being transparent. 
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/50434723b39055b58fbd61b141d97173dbea3a12">504347</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>August 10, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-alpha03</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-alpha03</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-alpha03</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/dd704c46b037e40efa784609230b5f62501f776f..bea814b246f89ff7244e3c6b0648f0b57e47897c/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a new outlined style for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chips</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Buttons</code> and new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">OutlinedButton</code> composables that provide a transparent <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/Button</code> with a thin border. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id597231272756493c4261f0aeb2d27357f64bb28">Id5972</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added overloads for modifying button shapes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icccdea3c8ac26d7ebacd38c2d6f4f4a88c225cbd">Icccde</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have corrected the size of the toggle control area of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> as it was not matching its UX spec. The UX Spec calls for a 4.dp spacer between the label and a 24x24.dp toggle control icon area giving a total 28.dp width. However the implementation is incorrectly giving 36x24.dp toggle control area. This results in taking away 8.dp of usable text label area. NOTE: This bug fix gives additional space for the text label and as result can (positively) impact the text layout for overflowing text. If you have screenshot tests including <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChips</code> they may need to be updated. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I514c858bd97dfedf860ac818dc27530a4a9e1a81">I514c8</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/240548670">b/240548670</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>July 27, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-alpha02</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-alpha02</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-alpha02</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/8094b683499b4098092c01028b55a38b49e357f2..dd704c46b037e40efa784609230b5f62501f776f/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have switched Compose for Wear OS dependencies on core Compose libraries from 1.2.0 to 1.3.0-alpha0X</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added overloads for modifying chip shapes (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I02e8759a2b4a0ecfb8a58ee3af02ee3d59801fc5">I02e87</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have animated the visibility of the vignette when showing/hiding Dialog, to be consistent with the existing scaling animation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ida33e5c2386ec4268bc64942f469b529ea754c44">Ida33e</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug where a divide-by-zero could occur with some fling behavior when scrolling. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I86cb623e42ad97bfda3382f58f1b525b73a6a595">I86cb6</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed a bug in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ChipDefaults.childChipColor()</code> to ensure that the disabled background color is fully transparent. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2b3c3ffdf046b9202e56411160ad41a51a1c6fb7">I2b3c3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/238057342">b/238057342</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.1.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.1.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.1.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>June 29, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.1.0-alpha01</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.1.0-alpha01</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.1.0-alpha01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/aa660d501ab7cf1ffb63464e855e86e650838fb6..8094b683499b4098092c01028b55a38b49e357f2/wear/compose">Version 1.1.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Picker&#39;s <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentDescription</code> parameter is now used only for the selected Picker option and takes a nullable String (previously, it was necessary to pass a mapping from option to the content description, but only the selected option was used). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ife6a7cb095c8e76ae2e6b7715e7efada12d971ec">Ife6a7</a>)</li>
<li>We have made accessibility improvements to Picker so that multi-picker screens are navigable with screen readers and the content description is accessible (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I64edb15386b8e92e4cc33b6a0bb816d333dba961">I64edb</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have updated the baseline profile rules packaged with the Wear Compose library (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9c69474e05395bb28ec62355714700b58923ba07">I9c694</a>)</li>
<li>We have corrected the direction of the gradient for Chips in right to left mode. Was top left-&gt;bottom right, is now top right-&gt;bottom left. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic2e77f4712f21f6b57cb7bbde63136b70769523e">Ic2e77</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the default gradients for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/ToggleChip/Card</code> to bring them in line with latest UX spec. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ChipDefaults.gradientBackgroundChipColors</code> has been updated to start from 50% of primary rather than 32.5%. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.cardBackgroundPainter</code> has been updated to start from 30% of primary and end at 20% of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSurfaceVariant</code> (was previously 20% to 10% <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSurfaceVariant</code>). <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip.toggleChipColors</code> changes from a linear gradient of 75% surface to 32.5% primary to 0% surface to 50% primary. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I43bbd9804f53013ea65f570bfdd91f9c5d2016f3">I43bbd</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a background color (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme.color.surface</code>) behind <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/ToggleChips</code> that have gradient backgrounds in order to ensure that they are properly visible in the unlikely event that a light color is used behind them. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibe1a442812a48a6d39912b4bbf399a2f4b11ae5b">Ibe1a4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/235937657">b/235937657</a>)</li>
<li>Picker items are now always center-aligned, fixing a bug when setting <code translate="no" dir="ltr">gradientRatio</code> to zero had the side-effect of changing the alignment. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I712b872a76103fa3365a2a8ef651394a2a0eab32">I712b8</a>)</li>
</ul>
