<h3 id="1.0.0" data-text="Version 1.0.0" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0</h3>

<p>July 27, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/baff514f1bfb244558d5b134ffe4f2eb582533f5..42400cf27f1a62feb94b39f90c9657094a898639/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Major features of 1.0.0</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>This is the first stable release of Compose for Wear OS (<a href="https://android-developers.googleblog.com/2022/07/compose-for-wear-os-10-stable.html">read more</a>).</li>
<li>Compose for Wear OS builds upon the core Compose libraries providing additional wearable-specific components and, where appropriate, alternate implementations of core Compose components tailored to wearable devices.</li>
<li>For a list of the key components in Wear Compose see the release notes for (<a href="https://developer.android.com/jetpack/androidx/releases/wear-compose#1.0.0-beta01">Compose for Wear OS Beta01</a>).</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have animated the visibility of the vignette when showing/hiding Dialog, to be consistent with the existing scaling animation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ida33e5c2386ec4268bc64942f469b529ea754c44">Ida33e</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug where a divide-by-zero could occur with some fling behavior when scrolling. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I86cb623e42ad97bfda3382f58f1b525b73a6a595">I86cb6</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed a bug in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ChipDefaults.childChipColor()</code> to ensure that the disabled background color is fully transparent. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2b3c3ffdf046b9202e56411160ad41a51a1c6fb7">I2b3c3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/238057342">b/238057342</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-rc02" data-text="Version 1.0.0-rc02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-rc02</h3>

<p>June 22, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-rc02</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-rc02</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-rc02</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/aa660d501ab7cf1ffb63464e855e86e650838fb6..baff514f1bfb244558d5b134ffe4f2eb582533f5/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-rc02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have corrected the direction of the gradient for Cards in right to left (RTL) mode. It was top left-&gt;bottom right, and it is now top right-&gt;bottom left. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic2e77f4712f21f6b57cb7bbde63136b70769523e">Ic2e77</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the default gradients for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/ToggleChip/Card</code> to bring them in line with the latest UX spec. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ChipDefaults.gradientBackgroundChipColors</code> has been updated to start from 50% of primary rather than 32.5%. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.cardBackgroundPainter</code> has been updated to start from 30% of primary and end at 20% of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSurfaceVariant</code> (was previously 20% to 10% onSurfaceVariant). <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip.toggleChipColors</code> changes from a linear gradient of 75% surface to 32.5% primary to 0% surface to 50% primary. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I43bbd9804f53013ea65f570bfdd91f9c5d2016f3">I43bbd</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a background color (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme.color.surface</code>) behind <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/ToggleChips</code> that have gradient backgrounds in order to ensure that they are properly visible in the unlikely event that a light color is used behind them. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibe1a442812a48a6d39912b4bbf399a2f4b11ae5b">Ibe1a4</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/235937657">b/235937657</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the baseline profile rules packaged with the Wear Compose library (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9c69474e05395bb28ec62355714700b58923ba07">I9c694</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-rc01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-rc01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-rc01</h3>

<p>June 15, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-rc01</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-rc01</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-rc01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/7cbb37cc779160b89644d03e042c129d0ce025d2..aa660d501ab7cf1ffb63464e855e86e650838fb6/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-rc01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Interfaces in compose libraries are now built using jdk8 default interface methods (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5bcf197603f66ec66177c98c01c3fe4868d60997">I5bcf1</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have removed the explicit call to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fillMaxWidth()</code> on list header as it is not needed and can result in problems if a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalinglazyColumn</code> has a mixture of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip()</code> components as the width will tend to grow/shrink as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ListHeader</code> items are scrolled in/out of view. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3714408eac2c75cd8168162ec94a600b0b87f024">I37144</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/235074035">b/235074035</a>)</li>
<li>We have fixed a bug in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> that could result in the list items not drawing correctly until scrolled if the 0th list item was large enough (including padding) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic6159b18937d97f9bb580cf59810880288ad6d4e">Ic6159</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/234328517">b/234328517</a>)</li>
<li>We have made a small adjustment in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> easing as items reach the edge of the screen to match UX spec updates. Old values <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CubicBezierEasing(0.25f, 0.00f, 0.75f, 1.00f)</code> -&gt; new values <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CubicBezierEasing(0.3f, 0f, 0.7f, 1f)</code>. To keep the old behavior you can override the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">scalingParams</code> of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie375ca83655ae09293b6565174787eac1e6b2e3e">Ie375c</a>)</li>
<li>We have added padding to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactChip</code> in order to ensure that its tap target size is at least 48.dp high to meet the Material accessibility guidelines. This might impact any layouts you have using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactChips</code> as they will be taking up additional space. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3d57caebc66e5d4c867f2ce19b4d0d9b5ebc9998">I3d57c</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-beta03" data-text="Version 1.0.0-beta03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-beta03</h3>

<p>June 1, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-beta03</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-beta03</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-beta03</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/6266a22ad9adaed6fa88fe98aa8adaa46eb96ccc..7cbb37cc779160b89644d03e042c129d0ce025d2/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-beta03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> work in Compose <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@Preview</code> mode. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3b3b61bd2c6bcec0fc8d440e677268c0363ccf4b">I3b3b6</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/232947354">b/232947354</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have changed the default value for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn.horizontalAlignment</code> property from Start to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CenterHorizontally</code> to ensure that when list items do not fill the entire width of the column they will be aligned for maximum visibility. To switch back to the previous behavior set <code translate="no" dir="ltr">horizontalAlignment = Alignment.Start</code>.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9ed4b6e01d8b4e6a24066c6ced54240f5a7cefff">I9ed4b</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Known Issues</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>CompactChip’s tap/touch height is smaller than Material accessibility guidelines. <em>This will be corrected in the next release (15th June)</em>. If you are using CompactChip this <em>will affect your layouts</em> as CompactChips will now have additional padding above and below. Please adjust and test your layouts or see the bug comments for a workaround to use the existing behavior. (<a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/234332135">b/234332135</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>New demo to animate adding or removing a start text on a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I16d75a1b694b50fb625b75a3301f335318d4490e">I16d75</a>)</li>
<li>Add tests for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPageIndicator.PagesState</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I64ed0ed5b41dd33c1426e7870afd6f96b45fe27c">I64ed0</a>)</li>
<li>Updating <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> closer to UX specs (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib7ea14c78be53fa46a1b5c66c09d7f6fa77d72d8">Ib7ea1</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-beta02" data-text="Version 1.0.0-beta02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-beta02</h3>

<p>May 18, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-beta02</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-beta02</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-beta02</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/53d512be6fd26bc30bffa7cae8e9769ec5c4bfbf..6266a22ad9adaed6fa88fe98aa8adaa46eb96ccc/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-beta02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Picker now always responds to scroll events even when in read-only mode. This avoids the need for users to first select a Picker by tapping, before they can scroll. In read-only mode, options other than that currently selected are obscured by a shim in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">gradientColor</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I72925a66999fa5ad1ec2307189483484aae4c9fc">I72925</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the UX behavior of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Chip/ToggleChip/CompactChip/SplitToggleChip</code> to stop them from doing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fillMaxWidth</code> by default. Instead they will grow to fit their contents. To keep the previous behavior simply add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()</code>(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I60a2cc1d2a7c1d88483ecbb374beae7fe4a688ff">I60a2c</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/232206371">b/232206371</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedTextStyle</code> constructor taking a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TextStyle</code> now also respects the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">fontWeight</code>(This may be added to the constructor and copy methods in future revisions of the API) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ieebb94f123e1b7d43b90249520bfaff7f62bb5c7">Ieebb9</a>)</li>
<li>Edge swiping improvements. When <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.edgeSwipeToDismiss</code>  is used and a swipe to the left is triggered from the edge area, it no longer triggers swipe-to-dismiss when swipe direction changes to the right. Previously, it was possible to trigger swipe-to-dismiss by swiping to the left  and then swiping to the  right.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I916eafd9eb308eca15d4925dc0490a93c5bbb830">I916ea</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPageIndicator</code> now shows up to 6 pages on the screen. If there are more than 6 pages in total, it shows a half-size indicator on the left or right, with a smooth transition between pages.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2ac2920a8f392233d44c6b739ea294fb29d5b80d">I2ac29</a>)</li>
<li>Improved default snap behavior on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Picker</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I495391b07b2cb92b3adcb6e23ae0153c2f176e78">I49539</a>)</li>
<li>Edge swiping improvements. When <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.edgeSwipeToDismiss</code> is used,  swipe-to-dismiss only triggers when first touch lands on the edge and  swiped to the right, Previously it was possible to trigger swipe-to-dismiss by swiping from any part of the screen if a scroll reaches the start.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8ca2a7eb6dd8f73d69de02e0d631c0cd672bfb5b">I8ca2a</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-beta01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-beta01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-beta01</h3>

<p>May 11, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-beta01</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-beta01</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-beta01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/c0a89ec374961b3015097ab307ebb8196dbe3888..53d512be6fd26bc30bffa7cae8e9769ec5c4bfbf/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-beta01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>What’s in Compose for Wear OS 1.0</strong></p>

<p>The <code translate="no" dir="ltr">1.0.0-beta01</code> of Compose for Wear OS marks an important milestone as the library is feature complete and the API locked.</p>

<p>Wear Compose Material components in the 1.0 release include:</p>

<ul>
<li>Material Theme - used as a replacement for the Compose for Mobile <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme</code>, provides the colors, shapes and typography for building components on Wearables that implement the Wear Material Design UX guidelines out of the box.</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code> - Button offers a single slot to take an icon, image or short text (3 characters max). Circular in shape with recommended sizes for default, large or small buttons. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> offers a single slot to take any content (icon, image or text) and is circular in shape with background size extra small. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> has optional transparent padding around the background that increases the clickable area. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code> is a button that offers a single slot to take any content (short text, icon or image) and has on/off (checked/unchecked) states with coloring and different icons to show whether checked or not</li>
<li>Cards - used to display information about applications such as notifications. Flexible design for different use cases with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AppCard</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TitleCard</code> giving different layouts and support for images as either card contents or backgrounds.</li>
<li>Chips - stadium shaped components similar to buttons, but with a larger area and multiple slots to allow for labels, secondary labels and icons. In different sizes and with support for images as backgrounds.</li>
<li>ToggleChips and SplitToggleChips - a Chip with a checked/unchecked state and the addition of a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleControl</code> slot to show an icon such as a switch or radio button to show the checked state of the component. In addition, the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code> has two tappable areas, one clickable and one toggleable.</li>
<li>CircularProgressIndicator - Wear Material progress indicator with two variations. The first expresses the proportion of completion of an ongoing task and supports a gap in the circular track between start and end angles. The second indicates indeterminate progress for an unspecified wait time.</li>
<li>curvedText - forms part of the DSL for describing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayouts</code>, along with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedRow</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedColumn</code>, to lay out components around circular devices. See Wear Component Foundation below for more details on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifier</code> (this plays a similar role to Modifiers in the non curved world and allows for configuration of various aspects of layout, padding, gradients, etc). </li>
<li>Dialog, Alert and Confirmation - Dialog displays a full-screen dialog, layered over any other content, and supports swipe-to-dismiss. It takes a single slot which is expected to be opinionated Wear Material dialog content such as Alert or Confirmation. Alert is opinionated dialog content with slots for icon, title and message. It has overloads for either two negative and positive buttons shown side-by-side or a slot for one or more vertically stacked chips. Confirmation is opinionated dialog content that displays a message for a given duration. It has a slot for an icon or image (that could be animated).</li>
<li>HorizontalPageIndicator - shows horizontal page position in a fashion appropriate to the Wearable form factor. Designed to take the full screen and show a curved indicator on round devices. Can be used with the Accompanist page viewer.</li>
<li>Icon - A Wear implementation of Icon which takes color and alpha from the Wear Material Theme. For a clickable icon, see Button or Chip.</li>
<li>Picker - displays a scrollable list of items from which to pick. By default, items will be repeated ‘infinitely’ in both directions. Can be displayed in read-only mode to hide unselected options.</li>
<li>PositionIndicator - shows scroll position or other positional indication in a fashion appropriate to the Wearable form factor. Designed to take the full screen and shows a curved indicator on round devices.</li>
<li>Scaffold - implements the basic Wear Material Design visual layout structure. This component provides an API to put together several Wear Material components (such as <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Vignette</code>) constructing the screen, ensuring proper layout strategy for them and collecting necessary data so these components will work together correctly.</li>
<li>ScalingLazyColumn - a scrolling scaling/fisheye list component that forms a key part of the Wear Material Design language. Provides scaling and transparency effects to the content items. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> is designed to be able to handle potentially large numbers of content items, which are only materialized and composed when needed.</li>
<li>Slider - allows users to make a selection from a range of values. The range of selections is shown as a bar, which can optionally be displayed with separators.</li>
<li>Stepper - a full-screen component that allows users to make a selection from a range of values, using increase/decrease buttons at the top and bottom of the screen, with a slot in the middle for Text or a Chip.</li>
<li>SwipeToDismissBox - handles the swipe-to-dismiss gesture. It takes a single slot for the background (only displayed during the swipe gesture) and the foreground content. Can optionally be combined with the androidx navigation library by using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> (see Wear Compose Navigation library below).</li>
<li>Text - A Wear implementation of the Compose Material Text component, taking color and alpha from the Wear Material Theme</li>
<li>TimeText - a component for showing Time and application status at the top of the screen. Adjusts to screen shape by using curved text on round screens.</li>
<li><p>Vignette - a screen treatment for use in the Scaffold that blurs top and bottom of screen when scrollable content is in use.</p></li>
<li><p>The following components are also included from Wear Compose Foundation:</p></li>
<li><p>CurvedLayout - Wear Foundation <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout</code> is a layout composable that places its children in an arc, rotating them as needed. This is similar to a Row layout curved into a segment of an annulus. Note that the content of a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout</code> is not a composable lambda - rather, it is a DSL (domain-specific language). All elements in the CurvedLayout’s DSL support an optional modifier parameter, created from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifier</code>.</p></li>
<li><p>basicCurvedText - an element in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout</code> DSL, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">basicCurvedText</code> allows developers to easily write curved text following the curvature of a circle (usually at the edge of a circular screen). <code translate="no" dir="ltr">basicCurvedText</code> can be only created within the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout</code> to ensure the best experience, like being able to specify the positioning, and using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifiers</code>. Note that in most cases curvedText should be used instead, since it uses Material theming.</p></li>
<li><p>curvedComposable - wraps normal composable content so that it can be used with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout</code>. If <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedComposable</code> has several elements inside, they will be drawn on top of each other (like a Box). To put several composables along a curve, wrap each one with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedComposable</code>.</p></li>
<li><p>curvedRow and curvedColumn - similar to Row and Column, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedRow</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedColumn</code> can be nested inside a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout</code> to lay elements out as needed. For a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedRow</code>, the angular layout direction and radial alignment may be specified. For a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedColumn</code>, the angular alignment and radial direction may be specified.</p></li>
<li><p>CurvedModifier - all curved components accept a modifier parameter that can be created using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifier</code>: background, size, weight and padding are supported.</p></li>
<li><p>The following component is also included from Wear Compose Navigation:</p></li>
<li><p>SwipeDismissableNavHost - provides a place in the Compose hierarchy for self-contained navigation to occur, with backwards navigation provided by a swipe gesture. Content is displayed within a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>, showing the current navigation level. During a swipe-to-dismiss gesture, the previous navigation level (if any) is shown in the background.</p></li>
<li><p>See previous release notes for the various Alpha releases for more details of what has been delivered.</p></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifier.padding*</code> functions. These are used to specify additional space to be added around a curved component.  (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4dbb48de80390332def76f830b1802167bd8df15">I4dbb4</a>)</li>
<li>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompositionLocal</code> internal class (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I424907fb374b6195dece35c591cc49665e7130c0">I42490</a>)</li>
<li>We have added constant values for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Button</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactButton</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleButton</code> icon sizes, as guidance
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I57cabdbbf3eb5fcfd2aabf2a4a9e78a0cf9dcf53">I57cab</a>)</li>
<li>Add enabled parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AppCard</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TitleCard</code>. Now they have a similar API to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.compose.material</code> Cards. When the parameter is set to false, the card will not be clickable. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idc48d9088b2f285ba2ecf541ec126f3a79ba7496">Idc48d</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/228869805">b/228869805</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Stepper now disables the decrease and increase buttons when the lower/upper limits have been reached (and applies ContentAlpha.disabled to the iconColor) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4be9fb53f859e20b4da89b2040f46d9bcf0e856e">I4be9f</a>)</li>
<li>We have added 1dp padding around Picker contents when drawn with a gradient to prevent jitter on text seen when swiping. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0b7b946c55a3553bd869a2d2add2958fd909a591">I0b7b9</a>)</li>
<li>Add screenshot tests for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5e8bc672f7a17e330b5d57f25fd4efc998a87632">I5e8bc</a>)</li>
<li>Add more tests for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AppCard</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TitleCard</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I85391f610a7ff821796a10cf94045d0c009c2803">I85391</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/228869805">b/228869805</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha21" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha21" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha21</h3>

<p>April 20, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha21</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha21</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha21</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/7ca43e00a517eaeeedc0a21f482b17f06e3d2181..c0a89ec374961b3015097ab307ebb8196dbe3888/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha21 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added new curved modifiers to specify the background of a curved element: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifier.background</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">.radialGradientBackground</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">.angularGradientBackground</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8f3921a9ac17280467ae8f2166e88fd0b2c5aea4">I8f392</a>)</li>
<li>Allow curved text overflow mode (clip/ellipsis/visible) to be specified. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8e7aa041f072d59eae87c9da0d5aee74a6d9fef1">I8e7aa</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifier.weight</code> modifier, similar to the one in Compose. This can be used on children of curvedRow and CurvedLayout (for width) and children of curvedColumn (for height). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8abbd06d6b444a4edd2a5c66bc0dd5d2a416978d">I8abbd</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifier.size</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">.angularSize</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">.radialSize</code> modifiers to specify the size of a curved element. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I623c71a99245a91f8cead2f25674487870d77ae9">I623c7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Reorder parameters to ensure background is before color consistently across the Wear Compose API (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4320831fdca3c14da7e1e1e290978afa5fcb5a5f">I43208</a>)</li>
<li>Removed clockwise &amp; <code translate="no" dir="ltr">insideOut</code> parameters and replaced with more expressive constants on new classes. Curved layout direction can now be <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LayoutDirection</code> aware, and it is inherited when not specified (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If0e6af67383a62a9e8135d5350b7f2b72fe79fda">If0e6a</a>)</li>
<li>We have replaced <code translate="no" dir="ltr">autoCenter: Boolean</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">autoCenter: AutoCentringParams</code> in order to fix an API issue with the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia9c90a1af9226e8c1510fd4199043a619554e85e">Ia9c90</a>)</li>
<li>We have renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">iconTintColor</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">toggleControlTintColor</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">iconColor</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">toggleControlColor</code> throughout the API (Chip/ToggleChip/Dialog/Slider/Stepper/...) as the color is applied to the icon/toggleControl slot. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ied23864a671b3cfd241cb0f077f111b762525a33">Ied238</a>)</li>
<li>Rewrite <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PageIndicatorStyle</code> enum into value class (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2dc72d7428a681586e2bf47a5bb40b449f43725a">I2dc72</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RowScope/ColumnScope/BoxScope</code> to some of the slots in our Composables to indicate to developers what the layouts assumptions are. This will allow developers to use additional modifiers on some slot content and avoid the need to provide extra layout elements. Additionally we have made some minor updates to the AppCard/TitleCard colors so that <code translate="no" dir="ltr">timeColor</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">appColor</code> default to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentColor</code>, these properties can still all be individually overridden if needed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I26b597bb6b2c9db3d8d3833a2dfa36374c7631a2">I26b59</a>)</li>
<li>Made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState.Companion</code> object private (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I39e84b8b16e9450f95147b44d4f10d40efa4cb8f">I39e84</a>)</li>
<li>Fix parameters order for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code>. A simple change to follow api guidelines (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I11fecebf74d60ccf4446e23935ca8e8724d7104a">I11fec</a>)</li>
<li>We have removed the Saver object for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState</code> as it was not used. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifb54eef912a95beb4b17f53eaf309c09c560bcac">Ifb54e</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CompactChip</code> to bring it inline with the latest UX Specification. Padding has been reduced to horizontal = 12.dp and vertical = 0.dp. The font for label has been changed from button to caption1. The recommended icon sizes are 20x20 when both icon and label are present and 24x24 for an icon only compact chip. For the icon only use case we have also ensured that the icon is center aligned. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iea2bef2ab11f750f9fe459c240354f06214f7930">Iea2be</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a number of new fields to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListLayoutInfo</code> to enable developers to know the amount of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentPadding</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">autoCenteringPadding</code> that has been applied. These can be useful for developers when calculating fling/scroll (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7577bc2830a0a5c2bbbb0d14a691e016c8f9dfc6">I7577b</a>)</li>
<li>We have implemented in/out transitions for Dialog. A <code translate="no" dir="ltr">showDialog</code> parameter has been added and the Dialog now controls its own visibility (this enables Dialog to run the intro and outro animations when the Dialog is shown/hidden). Note that the outro animation is not performed when the user leaves the dialog via swipe-to-dismiss. We have also added a default value for state in the recently added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> overload. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I682a03ea9354ed112f2b5be15634b27c41c6f31a">I682a0</a>)</li>
<li>In order to better support i18n and a11y we have changed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code> so that they no longer have a default for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">toggleControl</code> slot. We have also changed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChipDefaults</code> so that the following methods now return ImageVector rather than Icon (note that as they no longer return @Composables they have changed to start with lower case), <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwitchIcon()-&gt;switchIcon()</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CheckboxIcon-&gt;checkboxIcon()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RadioIcon()-&gt;radioIcon()</code> - this allows and encourages developers to create their own <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Icon()</code> composables with an appropriate <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentDescription</code> set. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5bb5b4158b2818130c314e4020249d96d4da59fb">I5bb5b</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHostState</code> parameter to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code>. This supports use of edge-swiping on screens used as navigation destinations, because <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState</code> can now be hoisted and used to initialize both <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHostState</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.edgeSwipeToDismiss</code> on screens that require edge-swiping. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I819f5f6daa7084f7c7b536652937d4d1dbdb7ff8">I819f5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/228336555">b/228336555</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Ensure curved layouts are updated when needed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie8bfa8217d76aea62d587074d1d67e0dfa2929a6">Ie8bfa</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/229079150">b/229079150</a>)</li>
<li>Bug fix for https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/226648931 (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia0a0aa4e2e480814665f0687af41506842f36de6">Ia0a0a</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/226648931">b/226648931</a>)</li>
<li>Removed unnecessary experimental annotations (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I88d7e4224b611bee3400db0d228e5c81dea7dab2">I88d7e</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha20" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha20" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha20</h3>

<p>April 6, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha20</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha20</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha20</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/5ef5671233460b844828e14a816255dbf7904868..7ca43e00a517eaeeedc0a21f482b17f06e3d2181/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha20 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">edgeSwipeToDismiss</code> modifier for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismiss</code>. Allows <code translate="no" dir="ltr">swipeToDismiss</code> to be active only on the left edge of the viewport. Used when the center of the screen needs to be able to handle horizontal paging, such as 2-d scrolling a Map or swiping horizontally between pages.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3fcec8831b68a87fde85251d0ac9895696b2ca85">I3fcec</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/200699800">b/200699800</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Base implementation of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifiers</code> , this opens the way to introduce ways to customize curved content (but no <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedModifiers</code> are provided yet, and the ability to create custom modifiers may be available later) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9b8df1a70179af00a2961b5c132bd1121d064b70">I9b8df</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">EdgeSwipe</code>modifier documentation and default values update for better understanding .(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6d00db6be4045798fcc5d33dca336f10d78dcf78">I6d00d</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PageIndicator</code> slot into Scaffold. By adding <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PageIndicator</code> directly into Scaffold we might assure that it will be correctly shown on circular devices. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia6042d3c52ba0e9785102a7a5eb293bca24f8704">Ia6042</a>)</li>
<li>Remove default Icons from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> and Stepper parameters. This will help developers to be more attentive to localization and accessibility requirements. Usages of default icons were shown in demos and samples.  (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7e6fda508ba23a2f16cd2bb381808711882fe48d">I7e6fd</a>)</li>
<li>Replace Trailing and Leading parameter names with Start and End in TimeText (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaac32655235950c786cc3bb2868434f63d5e2542">Iaac32</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> overload with an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onDismissed</code> parameter to support the common usage of triggering a navigation event when the swipe gesture has completed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I503534f8d11045c9446e976764134c05e147ea33">I50353</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/226565726">b/226565726</a>)</li>
<li>Removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExperimentalWearMaterialApi</code> annotations from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> usage (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ide5203259e9f1ff6b35074819aff59617e615c63">Ide520</a>)</li>
<li>We have marked <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyList/Column</code> scope and info interfaces as sealed as they are not intended for external developers to implement and this will allow us to add new members in them in future without binary breaking changes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7d99fb4b2281cf244d495278785d66e2bc1be6b7">I7d99f</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">flingBehaviour</code> property to the Picker and a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerDefaults.flingBehaviour()</code> method to enable configuration of the fling behavior such as adding RSB support. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerState</code> now implements the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScrollableState</code> interface. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib89c7f79787935382ae1bdf3b373f49ee09db29b">Ib89c7</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Update the Android Runtime (ART) baseline profile rules for Wear Compose libraries. ART can leverage profile rules on devices in order to compile ahead-of-time a specific subset of the application to improve the performance of the application. Note that this will have no effect on debuggable applications. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaa8efbbef602239ac422244ebb9b448c7eb5f18a">Iaa8ef</a>)</li>
<li>Improve documentation (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2c0514c3c40169a96d693a39a98b7d0be8c386bf">I2c051</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha19" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha19" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha19</h3>

<p>March 23, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha19</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha19</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha19</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/33cb12e8aba043a05b40470a5ef3be1b35114fd5..5ef5671233460b844828e14a816255dbf7904868/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha19 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedRow</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CurvedLayout</code>, and reworked to be a scope with a DSL. Using this DSL, more complex curved layouts can be specified using a series of nested <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedRow</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedColumn</code> (Which are the curved layout equivalents of Row and Column). Inside these layout elements, three elements can be used: <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedComposable</code> (to add any @Composable), <code translate="no" dir="ltr">basicCurvedText</code> (foundation&#39;s curved text) and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">curvedText</code> (wear material aware curved text). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ib776ab1e37f11a89cb1d1176a6790f3538e19132">Ib776a</a>)</li>
<li>Make the side for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> configurable. The basic PositionIndicator’s position can now be configured to be End (layout direction-aware),  OppositeRsb (takes into account screen rotation, to position itself opposite to the physical RSB), or the absolutes Left &amp; Right. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2f1f3150c8a80a79491c670779925308d587b3c1">I2f1f3</a>)</li>
<li>For <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code>, we have renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissTarget</code>.Original to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissValue.Default</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissTarget.Dismissal</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissValue.Dismissed</code>. We have also moved <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxDefaults.BackgroundKey</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxDefaults.ContentKey</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissKeys.Background</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissKeys.Content</code> respectively. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I47a36f46bd91b01795e99632837b5c3aa1224f39">I47a36</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a read-only mode to Picker, for screens with multiple Pickers where only one Picker is editable at a time. When the Picker is read-only, it displays the currently selected option, and a label if one has been provided. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I879de7842a21d000d5a2554922be976899f930d3">I879de</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState</code> has been refactored to restrict the scope of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ExperimentalWearMaterialApi</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.swipeable</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeableState</code>, which are now used internally. <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBoxState</code> now has <code translate="no" dir="ltr">currentValue</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">targetValue</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">isAnimationRunning</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">snapTo</code> members to support common use cases - please let us know if you require any further properties to be made available. Also fixed the behavior of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeableState</code> in the case where the swipe offset is within a rounding error of an anchor. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I58302544971da7b904a0b5681c06aae8e3f2ce3f">I58302</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Simplified and fixed code to detect if the content of a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> can be scrolled (used to decide if we display a
scrollbar or not) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7bce01d7becc03cd6a77ea1a0056002c30e86dde">I7bce0</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed a bug on Position Indicator when used with more than one state and switching between them (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I320b52abbc7649022385ac33919f6e59f92c4f4b">I320b5</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the default Compose for Wear OS theme typography/fonts to match our latest UX guidance. Of note display1 (40.sp) and display2 (34.sp) are now smaller than their previous values and various other minor updates to line height and line spacing have been made. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie3077b2941510a5cff490fb93a3a9e90fffc49ba">Ie3077</a>)</li>
<li>We have added resistance to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> so that motion only happens when swiping to dismiss and not at all in the opposite direction. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ifdfb90bb5577e5d36dde482eb303e08b9ad7e989">Ifdfb9</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed some of the default parameter values for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CircularProgressIndicator</code> functions to bring them in-line with Wear Material Design UX guidance. For the Spinner/Indeterminant version the size (40-&gt;24.dp), indicatorColor (primary-&gt;onBackground), trackColor transparency (30%-&gt;10%) and stroke width (4-&gt;3dp) have been updated. For the Progress/Determinate version the trackColor transparency (30%-&gt;10%) has been updated. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I659cc0bc67125d0af3a502ac5fd76d08d99de07c">I659cc</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the default scaling params of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> in-line with the latest Wear Material Design UX specifications. Visually this results in list items starting to be scaled closer to the list center, but being less scaled at the list edge than before. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ica8f35ee3860ef8ab48d71a52fb28383597b2ecb">Ica8f3</a>)</li>
<li>Some adjustments to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumnDefaults.snapFlingBehavior</code> to improve the end of the animation (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If32603e8effd6429c99021492321063212059b40">If3260</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha18" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha18" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha18</h3>

<p>March 9, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha18</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha18</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha18</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9b2b3d8efd5f00bd4af903bbaa926f6a712d0bd8..33cb12e8aba043a05b40470a5ef3be1b35114fd5/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha18 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Several improvements to PositionIndicator:  ShowResult
renamed PositionIndicatorVisibility. Some performance improvements to  avoid recomputations when not  needed (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iaed9d031fd5e881936abf420f77708e8c34efa66">Iaed9d</a>)</li>
<li>The recommended coloring for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code> has been updated. SplitToggleChip&#39;s now have a solid colored background when checked or unchecked with the coloring of the ToggleControl being the primary indication of whether the component is checked or not. We have added a new <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleDefaults.splitToggleChipColors()</code> to support the new color scheme. We have also simplified the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">toggleChipColors()</code> methods removing the splitBackgroundOverlayColor (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7e66e3c9a7c74b588edd7db9bca22f807aca68fc">I7e66e</a>)</li>
<li>We have added unadjustedSize to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListItemInfo</code> as it is not safe to calculate the original item size using the scaled size and scaling factor due to float maths precision. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I54657254014989469bed08b6ef3859cab814b826">I54657</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/221079441">b/221079441</a>)</li>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">HorizontalPageIndicator</code>. It represents a total number of pages and a selected page. Might be linear or curved, depending on the shape of the device. It also supports custom indicator shape, which defines how each indicator is visually represented. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iac8984eb938e64816850c494ffcaa7988e724cc8">Iac898</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerState</code> so that the numberOfOptions can be updated. This supports use-cases such as a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">DatePicker</code>, when the number of days in the month changes depending on the month selected. The constructor parameter for PickerState has changed to initialNumberOfOptions accordingly. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iad066cbe48265179e09cf17401e4a42344e09f5d">Iad066</a>)</li>
<li>Hide the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> when is a scrollbar and can&#39;t
scroll. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id0a7f131164666f81a95ca4ac1c98a68ec4f7b0f">Id0a7f</a>)</li>
<li>For consistency with Scaffold, our full-screen Dialog component now displays a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> and a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Vignette</code>. We are also now using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> instead of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Column</code>, which means that the Dialog contents are now in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListScope</code> (and typically need to be enclosed by item { /* content */ }). Dialog supports the verticalArrangement parameter accordingly. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idea13159860bce107a0bf2bd492fabfc575038fb">Idea13</a>)</li>
<li>We have changed the name of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ToggleChip</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SplitToggleChip</code> toggleIcon property to toggleControl to better align with Material Design in order to help designers and developers navigate the API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If59219f736c95c54c253f52217335204648364fa">If5921</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/220129803">b/220129803</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a new entry caption3 to the Wear Material Theme Typology.Caption3 is a small font used for the extra long-form writing like legal texts. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I74b133e3dbb660adf576893cfedf7bec95042c9b">I74b13</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/220128356">b/220128356</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Stop the snapping animation when we are there. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idb69dab09b454f70e59c00492da5db90706f9198">Idb69d</a>)</li>
<li>Animate changes in PositionIndicator. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I94cb921143f659c44dd166fe0882805ee5e809c5">I94cb9</a>)</li>
<li>Based on UI/UX feedback we have changed the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> autoCentering so that it will provide only enough space to make sure the items with index <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState.initialCenterItemIndex</code> or higher will be able to be fully scrolled to the center of the viewport. This allows developers to place one or two items about the item initially in the center which are not scrollable into the middle. This will mean that an autoCenter&#39;ing <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> will not be able to scroll above the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">initialCenterItemIndex/initialCenterItemScrollOffset</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I22ee2c5d2218cb89b3abfcc474386c26a424430f">I22ee2</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a demo for a Date Picker and fixed a bug in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerState</code> where the initiallySelectedOption was not applied until the Picker had been displayed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id0d7efdace5625690e444432de7bc2416fce551b">Id0d7e</a>)</li>
<li>In order to reduce the clipping of wider <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> items on circular screens we have increased the default horizontal content padding from 8 to 10 dp. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0d6098cb6bb07ea9b0a1c3e1eac4348543ca24ab">I0d609</a>)</li>
<li>Ensure the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PositionIndicator</code> is shown when scrolling. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ied9a23dfb565cefc46486ca3cd16bf0c5984a32e">Ied9a2</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha17" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha17" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha17</h3>

<p>February 23, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha17</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha17</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha17</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/db2ecbef194afcddfaede22e1d884a8959a9277c..9b2b3d8efd5f00bd4af903bbaa926f6a712d0bd8/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha17 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added snap support that can be used with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code>. Set <code translate="no" dir="ltr">flingBehavior = ScalingLazyColumnDefaults.flingWithSnapBehavior(state)</code> to enable snap support. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I068d3131c38b413df242977c708698bb32047394">I068d3</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/217377069">b/217377069</a>)</li>
<li>We have added demos for Picker used to
  select a time in either 24 hour or 12 hour clock. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie5552f6989293090c99e659823765e224fe589a9">Ie5552</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fix an issue with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TimeText</code> custom fonts &amp; styles on square device (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iea76ec7f02d57211b2455abbad36199f483b39b8">Iea76e</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListLayoutInfo</code> now has <code translate="no" dir="ltr">reverseLayout</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">viewportSize</code> and orientation properties matching those from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyListLayoutInfo</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4f2581c8e4c85d3530b428de6ca7d3088de439ca">I4f258</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/217917020">b/217917020</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> now has a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">userScrollEnabled</code> property matching that from <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyList</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I164d091a910d47c6a2a1297264b053a32e12b406">I164d0</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/217912513">b/217912513</a>)</li>
<li>Pickers now have a gradient on the top and bottom by default (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iab92ab2f2776a3cb28938861824a6611ec9298da">Iab92a</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have modified <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> so that it no longer greedily fills all of the space in its parent. Instead it will take its size from the size of its contents. This makes it consistent with the behaviour of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code>. If you want to reinstate the old behaviour then pass <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.fillMaxWidth()/width()/widthIn()</code> to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I51bf811c2e31e8dd797634e3ce42f7ce9805d79c">I51bf8</a>)</li>
<li>We have improved the exception message in <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost.kt</code> that was triggered if the navigation backstack was empty. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1b1dc975025dae2e49536a6ab04eb36233592d17">I1b1dc</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha16" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha16" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha16</h3>

<p>February 9, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha16</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha16</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha16</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/9dceceb54300ed028a7e8fc7a3454f270337ffde..db2ecbef194afcddfaede22e1d884a8959a9277c/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha16 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CircularProgressIndicator</code>. Progress indicators display the length of a process or an unspecified wait time.  Supports a gap (cutout) for TimeText or other components if used full-screen.
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iab8daa0e5355391bc09d78690d4690e489f7621c">Iab8da</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Pickers now have a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">flingBehavior</code> parameter, the default value makes them snap to the closest option when scrolling/flinging. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I09000fa7ce9e02b5bd75d3ddfc278e04bb5c547c">I09000</a>)</li>
<li>Additional integer API for InlineSlider and Stepper (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1b5d66881cec976f5d2c2c3fb272f9eabd5a8ddd">I1b5d6</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have changed the default initialCenterItemIndex for the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState</code> from 0-&gt;1. This means that unless overridden on state construction with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState.rememberScalingLazyListState(initialCenterItemIndex =</code><value><code translate="no" dir="ltr">)</code> then the 2nd list item (index == 1) will be placed in the center of the viewport at initialization and the 1st (index == 0) item will be placed before it. This allows for a better default visual effect out of the box as most of the viewport will be filled with list items. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I0c62304ff98c3233e48f38a3641ef856491b5838">I0c623</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/217344252">b/217344252</a>)</li>
<li>We have reduced the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> default <code translate="no" dir="ltr">extraPadding</code> that is provided to ensure that there are plenty of list items to draw (even when we are scaling some of them down in size) from 10% to 5%. This will avoid composing extra list items that might not appear in the viewport. If non standard scalingParams are being used (more extreme scaling for instance) the developer can adjust extra padding using <code translate="no" dir="ltr">viewportVerticalOffsetResolver</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I76be4dff5489bc7c07e3a1c0b2857ba4edf9f6bd">I76be4</a>)</li>
<li>Fix an issue with TimeText on multiple lines on square device (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibd3fbea3a09e9bd1871e8fb153bd2d72658ad3d7">Ibd3fb</a>)</li>
<li>We have modified <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> so that it no longer greedily fills all of the space in its parent. Instead it will take its size from the size of its contents. This makes it consistent with the behavior of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">LazyColumn</code>. If you want to reinstate the old behavior then pass <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.fillMaxSize()</code> to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> - NOTE: This change is incomplete and will be addressed in a follow up change in the next Alpha release.  (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I3cbfa038e71a6137d052fa5f41224df1563d5bd7">I3cbfa</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha15" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha15" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha15</h3>

<p>January 26, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha15</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha15</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha15</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f09f3e0f47cacc65a631115deac08ee8cc132ceb..9dceceb54300ed028a7e8fc7a3454f270337ffde/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha15 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a new property <code translate="no" dir="ltr">autoCentering</code> to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code>. When true (the default) this will ensure that all items including the first and last can be scrolled so that they are visible in the center of the lists viewport. Note that if using auto-centering you will probably want to set vertical content padding to 0.dp. If both autoCentering and vertical content padding are provided then they will both result in additional space being available before the first and after the last list items allowing them to be scrolled even further. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2a2827ad79ea6cf1cb5d9a623b600417def9cc2f">I2a282</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/214922490">b/214922490</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Dialog</code> component that enables any composable to trigger a full screen dialog that sits on top of other content. When shown, the dialog supports swipe-to-dismiss and will show its parent&#39;s content in the background during the swipe gesture. The dialog content is expected to be <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Alert</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Confirmation</code> (renamed from earlier components <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AlertDialog</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ConfirmationDialog</code>) - <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Alert</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Confirmation</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Dialog</code> are all in the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose.material.dialog</code> package. Alert and Confirmation can be used as navigation destinations. Also, added ColumnScope to Alert and Confirmation parameters as necessary. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia90143b7a387f4197861e0a1a338970692d4e057">Ia9014</a>)</li>
<li>We have removed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSurfaceVariant2</code> from the Compose for WearOS Material Theme Colors and replaced uses in the library with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">onSurfaceVariant</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Icd592e345414f0f9d4901578d761a20556777686">Icd592</a>)</li>
<li>Added a method to programmatically select an option on the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerState</code>, the initially selected option can now also be specified when creating a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">PickerState</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I92bdf1ba853a6f53ff1264dbdbe6b4d0f6128941">I92bdf</a>)</li>
<li>We have added support for customizing the fling behavior of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I1ad2e27966d6fbd84ce3c226b42729cbe47db1af">I1ad2e</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/208842968">b/208842968</a>)</li>
<li>We have added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavController.currentBackStackEntryAsState()</code> to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Wear.Compose.Navigation</code> library. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If90286c7debe623df926a091f15766abf04f2ecc">If9028</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/212739653">b/212739653</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.onRotaryScrollEvent()</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Modifier.onPreRotaryScrollEvent()</code> for Wear devices with a rotating side button.(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I18bf59262881d9c4a2edea159751164340ac3ed5">I18bf5</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/210748686">b/210748686</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha14" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha14" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha14</h3>

<p>January 12, 2022</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha14</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha14</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha14</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/301586664b5aad60548f21866cad502d524dbf9f..f09f3e0f47cacc65a631115deac08ee8cc132ceb/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha14 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p>We have added a number of methods to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListState</code> to allow developer control over scrolling to specific list items and also setting the initial list item and offset.</p>

<p>As part of this change we have also modified the ScalingLazyList so that it is oriented around the center of the viewport of the ScalingLazyList rather than the start of the viewport.</p>

<p>A new property <code translate="no" dir="ltr">anchorType: ScalingLazyListAnchorType = ScalingLazyListAnchorType.ItemCenter</code> has been added to the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyList</code> to control whether the center (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListAnchorType.ItemCenter</code>) or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Edge</code> (<code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListAnchorType.ItemStart</code>) should be aligned to the viewport&#39;s centerline.</p>

<p>As a result the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListItemInfo.offset</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyListItemInfo.adjustedOffset</code> have changed and will now reflect the offset of the item with respect to both the position of the list item and the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">anchorType</code> of the list. E.g. for a <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ScalingLazyColumn</code> with <code translate="no" dir="ltr">anchorType</code> of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ItemCenter</code> and an list item positioned with its center on the centerline of the viewport the offset would be <code translate="no" dir="ltr">0</code>.</p>

<p>The new methods are <code translate="no" dir="ltr">scrollTo</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">animatedScrollTo</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">centerItemIndex</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">centerItemOffset</code>.
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I61b61fbed9539408138216fb9acef46c9bd94479">I61b61</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>We have added a back button handler to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code>, so that pressing back navigates to the previous level in the navigation hierarchy. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5b08689b1651c1aae5f038f058956007df398909">I5b086</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/210205624">b/210205624</a>)</p></li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha13" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha13" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha13</h3>

<p>December 15, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha13</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha13</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha13</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/75784ce6dbac6faa5320e5898e9472f02ab8710c..301586664b5aad60548f21866cad502d524dbf9f/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha13 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have made <code translate="no" dir="ltr">RangeIcons</code> internal (referenced internally by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">InlineSlider</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code>). (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I927ec058650a49adb0bf5603410b962c025446bc">I927ec</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p>Fixed an issue where <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> would add a destination to the Compose hierarchy before it has reached the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CREATED</code> Lifecycle state, resulting in an <code translate="no" dir="ltr">IllegalStateException</code>. This fix was a prerequisite to updating dependency on <code translate="no" dir="ltr">navigation-compose</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">2.4.0-beta02</code> and beyond. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I40a2ba51ec8805007dd11f531a5807e60f595a0d">I40a2b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/207328687">b/207328687</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Added a Drawables enum class for getting drawable resources within the Wear Compose library, so that reflection is no longer needed. This fixes a bug where library drawables were removed when <code translate="no" dir="ltr">minifyEnabled=true</code> or <code translate="no" dir="ltr">shrinkResources=true</code>).
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/q/Ib2a98513706c9d2ec080498742ae6d6810ae6be3">Ib2a98</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Added tests for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Stepper</code> in Wear Compose (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I2d03a3e12fe55d6f98fa9be31a4f8511e8ca69b2">I2d03a</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>Added samples for <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> in Wear Compose Navigation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I85f063563bd521badf131943dbe49754a408c153">I85f06</a>)</p></li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha12" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha12" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha12</h3>

<p>December 1, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha12</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha12</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha12</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/cc1240d00b28657ee0c1a937f60430eaf1b03b09..75784ce6dbac6faa5320e5898e9472f02ab8710c/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha12 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p>We have added a Stepper component which allows users to make a selection from a range of values. Stepper is a full-screen control with increase and decrease buttons at the top and bottom, and a slot in the middle (expected to take either a Chip or Text). The button icons can be customized if required. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I625fe06a1b1e90d1e59cb20be9fc5b8b19f387bf">I625fe</a>)</p></li>
<li><p>We have added 2 new composables for displaying dialogs:
AlertDialog waits for a response from the user and displays a title, icon, message and either a) two buttons for simple positive/negative choices or b) vertically stacked chips or toggle chips for more flexible choices,
ConfirmationDialog displays an acknowledgement with a timeout. This simple dialog has slots for a title and an (animated) icon. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic2cf88647bf55c8c93d7b3d8140249c98af0ccbb">Ic2cf8</a>)</p></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add units (millis) to suggested dialog duration values. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I09b484c76b9c4f3291b1fdd5024340fef95d377b">I09b48</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha11" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha11" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha11</h3>

<p>November 17, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha11</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha11</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha11</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/f07d12061370a603549747200c79b60239706330..cc1240d00b28657ee0c1a937f60430eaf1b03b09/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha11 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added a picker component that lets the user select an item from a scrolling list. By default, the list of selectable items is repeated &#39;infinitely&#39; in both directions, to give the impression of a rotating cylinder seen from the side. Two features will be added in later releases: snapping to a value after a swipe/fling; adding a function to PickerState to set/scroll to the current value.
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6461b07145e55d7e3d5f9db6653227d0f9670d75">I6461b</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added a ScalingLazyItemScope and some new modifiers fillParentMaxSize/fillParentMaxWidth/fillParentMaxHeight to allow list items to be sized based on the size of the parent container. Items can be set to fill all or a fraction of the parent’s size. This exposes functionality already available in the LazyRow/Column (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4612f5088090567fe9fcec598ffbd04642fa9aa5">I4612f</a>)</li>
<li>Added support to ScalingLazyColumn to allow items to have a key. Also added convenience methods to allow adding of items from Arrays and Lists. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic1f89a6c4ffd58f6e5a043e4148fe6f7fdc130f9">Ic1f89</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Additional examples for TimeText (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I8cb64484b2b15756bc155aa642418cdb4791709e">I8cb64</a>)</li>
</ul>
