<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha09" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha09" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha09</h3>

<p>October 27, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha09</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha09</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha09</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/db0888af4fa9a8eaeaf55cc1f120724bc67bdb20..b5f9c6b124ab46a4c5eee7f15d2443287f8a539d/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha09 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have launched the Developer Preview of Compose on Wear OS - see our <a href="https://android-developers.googleblog.com/2021/10/compose-for-wear-os-now-in-developer.html">blog post</a> which reviews the main composables and links to further resources to starting using them.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added support for developers to be able to customize all of the colors in the Wear Material Design Color theme. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4759baf83e4f76138fd3769a1292ebe5da927b21">I4759b</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/199754668">b/199754668</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added SwipeToDismissBox samples that persist state (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ibaffe1d598d15c8b4105f7455ade42628b481c56">Ibaffe</a>)</li>
<li>Added links to developer.android.com guides from KDocs for CurvedText, TimeText and
SwipeToDismissBox. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I399d4c3ba7fe520772c3746da17080907ac764cf">I399d4</a>)</li>
<li>SwipeDismissableNavHost now throws if there&#39;s no current destination (indicates that
the NavGraph was not built with the wear.compose.navigation.composable
utility function) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I91403cb5ce05de34a522dccb5e380c356b496e31">I91403</a>)</li>
<li>Added additional documentation and examples for time source usage in TimeText (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4f6f0b374b8bbef5080569b3942c7760be46781a">I4f6f0</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha08" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha08" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha08</h3>

<p>October 13, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha08</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha08</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha08</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1f6bc4d47b7be46a5af151ed726e84db0a1cf9f9..db0888af4fa9a8eaeaf55cc1f120724bc67bdb20/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha08 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have renamed AppCard and TitleCard <code translate="no" dir="ltr">body</code> properties to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">content</code> and moved them to the end of the property list to allow them to be provided as a trailing lambda. Also renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">bodyColor</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">contentColor</code> for consistency with the new slot names. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I57e78a7565904d5c32f7ee39888ea48bcf3478e8">I57e78</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added links to developer.android.com
guides from KDocs for button, card, chip, theme,
position indicator and scaling lazy column components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I22428bd80dbfb5730d834880ca4575679129e6da">I22428</a>)</li>
<li>Fix WearOS SwipeToDismissBox sometimes not handling swipes. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9387e6584e9d04d7ffda3a4319e3da2da13788b5">I9387e</a>)</li>
<li>Added samples for Button, CompactButton,
Chip, CompactChip, AppCard, TitleCard,
ToggleButton, ToggleChip, SplitToggleChip (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iddc15f775b02598716517ecca66d92d82416a035">Iddc15</a>)</li>
<li>Added microbenchmark performance tests for
Card, Chip, ToggleChip, TimeText and ScalingLazyColumn. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If2fe9ad7e36e89ef96fb7310ae359386ec8c6f1b">If2fe9</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha07" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha07" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha07</h3>

<p>September 29, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha07</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha07</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha07</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1a3dcfb231517d6104969f17063fcc6c97ba6eeb..1f6bc4d47b7be46a5af151ed726e84db0a1cf9f9/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha07 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added a CurvedText component in material, a component allowing developers to easily write curved text following the curvature of a circle (usually at the edge of a circular screen).
(<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I19593cf0f2b84d7b9f5f212a43ba61592604d696">I19593</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added tests for TimeText (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idfead382f43fa40bcfffbe4cda4226260a61ca70">Idfead</a>)</li>
<li>Transform ArcPaddingValues into an interface. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Iecd4c7061fc380b4d4b089d12c982be70d9ec59f">Iecd4c</a>)</li>
<li>Added animation to SwipeToDismissBox (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9ad1b2d18112932681cc05a0daaf6a5cf5682e60">I9ad1b</a>)</li>
<li>Added hasBackground parameter to the SwipeToDismissBox
API so that the swipe gesture can be disabled when there
is no background content to display. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I313d86797efcef05eaf9d5ef4d86ae1b0c761a17">I313d8</a>)</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberNavController()</code> now takes a optional
set of <code translate="no" dir="ltr">Navigator</code> instances that will be added to the
returned <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavController</code> to better support optional
Navigators such as those from
<a href="https://google.github.io/accompanist/navigation-material/">Accompanist Navigation Material</a>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4619e6c4b47fc76c45a64c68085519fd8d18f699">I4619e</a>)</li>
<li>Reference NamedNavArgument from
navigation-common and remove copy from
wear.compose.navigation. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I43af6b58f3d508619fd55cc6615f7edba8d3e1c8">I43af6</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Fixed CurvedRow test flakiness on smaller devices. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/If7941323c02917d3cf5355bc41c893d16639c92f">If7941</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed possible flickering on CurvedRow when the content updates,
and ensures the curved row is remeasured (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie4e06fa0f9a7cc74b5c5a22cdc133091a6591990">Ie4e06</a>)</li>
<li>ChipDefaults.gradientBackgroundChipColors() has been updated in line with UX Spec changes. The gradient now starts with MaterialTheme.colors.primary with alpha 32.5% and ends with MaterialTheme.colors.surface with alpha @ 0% over a background of MaterialTheme.colors.surface @ 75% alpha. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id1548a3032807886b9ae5d8ff2f50a3ccc07e658">Id1548</a>)</li>
<li>We have updated the colors for ToggleChips when in the selected state to match the latest Wear Material Design UX Spec guidance. When selected ToggleChips now have a gradient background from MaterialTheme.color.surface @ 0% alpha, top left, to MaterialTheme.color.primary @ 32% alpha, bottom right, over a background of MaterialTheme.color.surface @ 75% alpha. This results in a more subtle difference between checked and unchecked for the ToggleChip. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Idd40b198511486abe037773008c23a731f055779">Idd40b</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha06" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha06" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha06</h3>

<p>September 15, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha06</code>, <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha06</code>, and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-navigation:1.0.0-alpha06</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1a3dcfb231517d6104969f17063fcc6c97ba6eeb/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha06 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have added Scaffold a top level application composable that provides a structure for handling PositionIndicators (like Scroll or Volume) position, an area at the top of the screen for displaying the time and application status, and also supports a Vignette to blur the screen top and bottom edge for scrollable content. The main area of the Scaffold is where the application contents are placed. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5e0bf5d3b7fe6ebc247a8b9ba255b00167fe35c4">I5e0bf</a>)</li>
<li>Added TimeText implementation for Wear Compose (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5654cc5c2e02a3eff5fd48317b5a8600d3b17644">I5654c</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Wear Compose Navigation Library</strong></p>

<ul>
<li><p>We have added the first release of the Wear Compose Navigation library, which provides integration between the Wear Compose and Androidx Navigation libraries. It provides a simple means to navigate between @Composable functions as the destinations in your application.</p></li>
<li><p>This initial release provides:</p>

<ul>
<li>A <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> composable that hosts a navigation graph and provides backwards navigation via swipe gestures</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">NavGraphBuilder.composable</code> extension to assist with constructing navigation graphs</li>
<li><code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberSwipeDismissableNavController()</code> to allow hoisting state</li>
</ul></li>
<li><p>Example usage where we create two screens and navigate between them:</p>
<div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Kotlin"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-kd">val</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nv">navController</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">rememberSwipeDismissableNavController</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">()</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">SwipeDismissableNavHost</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">composable</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s">"start"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">        </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Column</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">            </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">horizontalAlignment</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Alignment</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-na">CenterHorizontally</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-w">            </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">modifier</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Modifier</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-na">fillMaxSize</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(),</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">        </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">            </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Button</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">onClick</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">navController</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-na">navigate</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s">"next"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">})</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">                </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Text</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s">"Go"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">            </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">        </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">composable</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s">"next"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">        </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Column</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">            </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">horizontalAlignment</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Alignment</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-na">CenterHorizontally</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">            </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">verticalArrangement</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Arrangement</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-na">Center</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">            </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">modifier</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Modifier</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-na">fillMaxSize</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(),</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">        </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">            </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Text</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s">"Swipe to go back"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">        </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></li>
<li><p>Wear Compose Navigation is packaged as a separate library so that simple WearCompose applications that implement their own hand-rolled navigation are not required to depend on the Androidx Navigation library.</p></li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissableNavHost</code> to support
<code translate="no" dir="ltr">rememberSaveable</code> by setting the key identity for background and content (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I746fd6214b2f58bee625a86fd3f422122a0528ed">I746fd</a>)</li>
<li>We have added a PositionIndicator adapter that can handle LazyListState (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I21b88fee904f4e63dfb8d9dcf305547c1e148f2b">I21b88</a>)</li>
<li>Updated SwipeToDismissBox to support rememberSaveable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie728bdfcb0d77b1098188009b57b7e0c21218ab5">Ie728b</a>)</li>
<li>We have added reverseLayout support to the ScalingLazyColumn. This allows for the reversing of the direction of scrolling and layout (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9e2fcb9d90e498d199224b9abad55dcf4bdf3068">I9e2fc</a>)</li>
<li>Deprecated <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performGesture</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">GestureScope</code>, which have
been replaced by <code translate="no" dir="ltr">performTouchInput</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">TouchInjectionScope</code>. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia5f3f740c51a1add60fa82189d583d8a5192dd31">Ia5f3f</a>, <a href="https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/190493367">b/190493367</a>)</li>
<li>We have renamed VignetteValue to VignettePosition and renamed VignetteValue.Both renamed to VignettePosition.TopAndBottom. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I57ad7bca7ceaaf0ff3f0341a691f78b94630dcbc">I57ad7</a>)</li>
<li>We have renamed ScalingLazyColumnState to ScalingLazyListState, ScalingLazyColumnItemInfo to ScalingLazyListItemInfo, ScalingLazyColumnLayoutInfo to ScalingLazyListLayoutInfo and ScalingLazyColumnScope to ScalingLazyListScope in case we decide to add a ScalingLazyRow implementation in the future. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I22734a2d2e5068935c7281007612e3fc088b4a88">I22734</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Updated CompactChip documentation to describe what happens if neither an icon nor a label is provided. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I4ba881d111185c316f39840f626d6f37f931b520">I4ba88</a>)</li>
<li>We have made some adjustments to the Wear card components. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I6b3d039916cae8f8dcda9306090ac127b771f0a8">I6b3d0</a>)
<ol>
<li>TitleCard spacing between Title and Body reduced from 8.dp to 2.dp.</li>
<li>TitleCard header font changed from body to title3.</li>
<li>Card background gradient changed to make the background appear darker.</li>
</ol></li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha05" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha05" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha05</h3>

<p>September 1, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha05</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha05</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/1e0ab9e58c3c2ebe8152b7507938aef7e9c1acdc..bf63d633b292368932b7ea1994e4116f95a94b5c/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha05 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Mark ArcPaddingValues as @Stable (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I57deba17572c7df792ed5db80eb70f0915e6fc3d">I57deb</a>)</li>
<li>ScalingLazyColumnState now implements the ScrollableState interface giving developers programmatic access to scroll the component. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I47dbcd941fd5b9c70f297245d2f4e5bd4eb81c96">I47dbc</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We have reduced the spacing between Icon and Text in Chip and ToggleChip to bring them in line with updates to the UX Spec. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I838026ae034d9e8b9a2c302647cc9d3d19ce653a">I83802</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha04" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha04" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha04</h3>

<p>August 18, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha04</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha04</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/d725303accfa9be6d5c3d61c7603ed1b9a780cbd..1e0ab9e58c3c2ebe8152b7507938aef7e9c1acdc/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha04 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added a SwipeToDismissBox and swipeable modifier that can be used to
support a left-to-right swipe-to-dismiss gesture.
Although independent of navigation components,
this is expected to be used to exit one screen and navigate to another. Added
integration tests to demo swipe-to-dismiss. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7bbaa6256c170c7e46cd9d7a8de5af0ea45d2a06">I7bbaa</a>)</li>
<li>We have added ScalingLazyColumnItemInfo and ScalingLazyColumnLayoutInfo interfaces to ScalingLazyColumnState class to enable developers to know the actual positions and sizes of items in the ScalingLazyColumn after scaling has been applied. We have also fixed a bug with the way that scaling was calculated when &#39;top&#39; content padding is applied to the ScalingLazyColumn. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I27c07d0048f076da4d30e3b602f86fa417f1f1f9">I27c07</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add CurvedTextStyle class to specify curved text styling
Options. Similar to TextStyle, but now only supports color, fontSize and background. More styling options will be added in the future. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I96ac3539ec781ecbbc00085c06d33e9cce014646">I96ac3</a>)</li>
<li>We have added ScalingLazyColumnItemInfo and ScalingLazyColumnLayoutInfo interfaces to ScalingLazyColumnState class to enable developers to know the actual positions and sizes of items in the ScalingLazyColumn after scaling has been applied. We have also fixed a bug with the way that scaling was calculated when &#39;top&#39; content padding is applied to the ScalingLazyColumn. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I27c07d0048f076da4d30e3b602f86fa417f1f1f9">I27c07</a>)</li>
<li>Added <code translate="no" dir="ltr">@ExperimentalWearMaterialApi</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeDismissTarget</code> enum, part of the <code translate="no" dir="ltr">SwipeToDismissBox</code> API. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I48b5e453dfac2f72517b56c26f398c74a1aeacc2">I48b5e</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added test material for SwipeToDismissBox (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I9febcf2ff228d7a2887e064ea9c587e7423db201">I9febc</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha03" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha03" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha03</h3>

<p>August 4, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha03</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha03</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/97264aa4532db7f7db1ffb3f42f3a9204971dbfc..d725303accfa9be6d5c3d61c7603ed1b9a780cbd/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha03 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added CurvedText component, that allows developers to easily write text following
the curvature a circle (usually at the edge of a circular screen) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id1267f2b4bc88780b7a91b77a51c31d3606fc9aa">Id1267</a>)</li>
<li>We have renamed <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.imageBackgroundPainter()</code> to <code translate="no" dir="ltr">CardDefaults.imageWithScrimBackgroundPainter()</code> to make it clear that the background image with have a scrim drawn over it. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I5320680f975d6ec32e00648b08f82c29cfc4884d">I53206</a>)</li>
<li>Adding ScalingLazyColumn component that provides a list component for Wear Material that gives a fisheye view with the list contents scaling down in size and becoming transparent as they scale towards the edge of the component. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7070cd6a7250352dc4d9c0a110a9e7468dc02c0a">I7070c</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>We changed the default color of the appName content in AppCard in response to a UX Spec update. The default color for the appName is now <code translate="no" dir="ltr">MaterialTheme.colors.onSurfaceVariant</code>. Additionally added a missing parameter doc description for the title slot. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ic4ad16cbf62de5c4ba89de1062c42b0025ec7db5">Ic4ad1</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha02" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha02" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha02</h3>

<p>July 21, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha02</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha02</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/19ae3a88ff0824d615355b492cb56049e16991f2..97264aa4532db7f7db1ffb3f42f3a9204971dbfc/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha02 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Added a new class CurvedRow to laid out composables in an arc (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I29941d2f915c3da65194402367dcd30898a4d0b2">I29941</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new type of card for use in applications (TitleCard), also add support for having images as the background to Cards to emphasize their contents (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I53b0f56021b718041832202707613b2e2667cd72">I53b0f</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>API Changes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add support for radial alignment to CurvedRow (similar to the
vertical alignment in a row) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id9de5375161076290a6ec3935724381f8fa8e403">Id9de5</a>)</li>
<li>Add a new class CurvedRow to laid out composables in an arc (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I29941d2f915c3da65194402367dcd30898a4d0b2">I29941</a>)</li>
<li>Added a new type of card for use in applications (TitleCard), also add support for having images as the background to Cards to emphasize their contents (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I53b0f56021b718041832202707613b2e2667cd72">I53b0f</a>)</li>
<li>Added toggle icons (checkbox, switch and radio buttons) to ToggleChipDefaults to make it easier for developers to configure ToggleChip and SplitToggleChips (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I7b6395b8daffdb656f5092e23af8a39196a5cbf6">I7b639</a>)</li>
<li>The start and end content padding for Chips has been updated so that it is consistently 14.dp regardless of whether the Chip has an icon present or not (was previously 12.dp if icon present and 14.dp if not) (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I34c8671e43deff8c262f5208c342de1859ce7ee6">I34c86</a>)</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></p>

<ul>
<li>Add tests for CurvedRow (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I93cdbc88ff3fcf8c87e8d51184b043abd9acbb14">I93cdb</a>)</li>
<li>Tying Wear Compose dependencies to Compose 1.0.0-rc01. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ie6bc96b55141518fe956d21119318db5734bd64f">Ie6bc9</a>)</li>
<li>Changed the handing of background image painting in Cards and Chips so that the image is Cropped rather than being stretched in order to maintain image proportions. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/I29b41e2dc4dcfc789e2349da986bc070eca9b874">I29b41</a>)</li>
<li>Added more demos and integration tests for Button and ToggleButton. (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Id6461620cb501d1108d2c24e0f0894014ffd9434">5e27ed2</a>)</li>
<li>Added more Chip tests to cover the content colors for imageBackgroundChips (<a href="https://android-review.googlesource.com/#/q/Ia9183927d1b1bd37da6e2b6a76498e7cbe320cf5">Ia9183</a>)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="1.0.0-alpha01" data-text="Version 1.0.0-alpha01" tabindex="-1">Version 1.0.0-alpha01</h3>

<p>July 1, 2021</p>

<p><code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-foundation:1.0.0-alpha01</code> and <code translate="no" dir="ltr">androidx.wear.compose:compose-material:1.0.0-alpha01</code> are released. <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+log/19ae3a88ff0824d615355b492cb56049e16991f2/wear/compose">Version 1.0.0-alpha01 contains these commits.</a></p>

<p><strong>New Features</strong></p>

<p>Wear Compose is a Kotlin, Compose-based library that supports Wear Material design, an extension of Material Design for WearOS wearables.  This first alpha release contains early, functional implementations of the following:</p>

<ul>
<li>Material theme - configures the colors, typography and shapes consistently across the components used from this library.</li>
<li>Chip, CompactChip - chips are stadium shaped and variations are available to take icon, label and secondary label content.</li>
<li>- ToggleChip, SplitToggleChip - a specialized type of chip that includes a slot for a bi-state toggle icon such as a radio button or checkbox. In addition, the SplitToggleChip has two tappable areas, one clickable and one toggleable.</li>
<li>Button, CompactButton - buttons are circular in shape, with a single content slot for an icon or minimal text (maximum 3 characters).</li>
<li>ToggleButton - a button that turns an action on or off, with a single slot for icon or minimal text (maximum 3 characters).</li>
<li>Card, AppCard - rectangular shaped with rounded corners, offering slots for content such as app icon, time, title and body.</li>
</ul>

<p>Future releases will extend the Widget set adding support for Wear Material Design pickers, sliders, lists, page indicators, dialogs, scroll  rsb indicators, toasts and more.</p>

<p>Additionally support will be provided for other Wearable Specific features such as curved layouts and text, as well as scaffolding to make it easy for developers to build Wearable apps/overlays.</p>

<p>Wear Compose Material is designed with the same principles as Compose Material, although being targeted at wearables. The Wear Compose Material library should be used in place of the Compose Material library when building for a Wearable device.</p>

<p>The two “Material” libraries should be considered mutually exclusive and should not be mixed in the same app. If developers find themselves including the Compose Material library in their dependencies it would suggest that either a) there are components missing from the Wear Compose Material library, please let us know what you need, or b) are using a component that we do not recommend for use on a Wearable Device.</p>
